No successor will be appointed for the time being. All routine matters will be handled by the chargé d'affaires. Tensions in Czech-Polish relations have existed for some time. Diplomatic circles believe that this move by the Czech government is a result of the current tensions in bilateral relations. (Kuomin News Agency dispatch on the 30th)

United States Expands Military Strength to Strengthen Defense and Cope with Contingencies, Army by 40,000, Navy by 10,000, Recruitment to Begin This Month 39

(Washington) Congress previously passed the next fiscal year's defense budget in April, approving appropriations of 860 million yuan, including plans to expand the army and navy. This will be implemented when the fiscal year begins on July 1st. The conscription office will handle the recruitment. It is estimated that 47,000 army personnel, 11,000 navy personnel, and 1,100 marines will need to be recruited. The army should complete this recruitment within three years, and the navy within four years. When the recruitment is completed in the future, the total number of new troops nationwide will be 165,000 for the army, 93,500 for the navy, and 16,000 for the marines. Although the number of army personnel has been increased, it is only to replenish the existing personnel of each unit and is not intended to establish new units. The newly recruited navy personnel will be assigned to the warships newly built this year (according to this year, the United States is building 24 warships). According to President Roosevelt's instructions, those who are members of the "Civilian Conservation Corps," established under the Works Progress Administration, may not be recruited, as these corps members were established to address the unemployment problem and should not be used to fill the ranks of the "regular army." (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

Eden Presents to the British House of Commons on the Experiences of Visiting Paris and Rome, Acts as Mediator on Italian-Ethiopian Issue, Expresses Regret That Suggestions Were Not Accepted, Three Countries Still Seek Ways to Cooperate 40

(London) Undersecretary of State Eden presented to the House of Commons today on the experiences of visiting Paris and Rome. He stated that the purpose of his trip was to sincerely explain the Anglo-German Naval Agreement to the French government and to discuss methods of proceeding with the matters mentioned in the London Communiqué of February 3, as well as to meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Mussolini stated that he could not accept the British suggestions regarding a final resolution of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. The British suggestion was that the United Kingdom cede a portion of British Somaliland to Ethiopia to provide access to the sea. The United Kingdom made this suggestion to facilitate any territorial and economic concessions that Ethiopia might make to Italy in the negotiated solution. The United Kingdom, in addition to seeking watering and grazing rights for tribes within any territories that Ethiopia might cede to Italy, did not wish to request any other concessions as compensation. The United Kingdom took this attitude not out of self-interest or to protect the interests of the British in Africa, but because the United Kingdom is a member of the League of Nations and is willing to resolve disputes. He told Mussolini that British foreign policy is based entirely on the League of Nations. The result of his talks with Mussolini and French Prime Minister Laval is that the three parties are currently seeking ways to cooperate in fulfilling the sections listed in the London Communiqué of February 3. There is now reason to hope that the best approach can be found in the near future. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

(Paris) A London correspondent for Le Matin analyzed the unease among British people regarding the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, stating in brief: "A proverb says that Egypt is the Nile, and the Nile is Egypt, which shows the importance of the Nile River to Egypt. However, the Nile River waterway is formed by the confluence of various water sources in the Ethiopian highlands. All the streams within Ethiopia flow towards Egypt, making Egypt a naturally rich country. Without the water source from Ethiopia, the Nile River waterway would be dry for a significant portion of the year. The Nile River is divided into two major tributaries, one is the Blue Nile, and the other is the White Nile. The Blue Nile originates from Lake Tana, flows through west-central Ethiopia, meanders into Anglo-Egyptian Sudan, and joins the White Nile. Therefore, in recent years, engineering experts have repeatedly designed to build dikes around Lake Tana to raise the water level of Lake Tana to prevent the Blue Nile's water source from drying up. Once the Lake Tana water dike project is completed, it will benefit the agricultural irrigation in the Blue Nile region no less than the famous dike built by the British in Aswan, Egypt. For this reason, if the country controlling the Blue Nile's water source can cooperate with other countries involved, the Anglo-Egyptian Sudan water conservancy will naturally not have to worry about being depleted. It is said that when British Lord Privy Seal Eden went to Rome, he suggested various plans to assist Italy in developing trade in Ethiopia. His intention was to protect the Blue Nile's water source, so he tried his best to seek Italy's understanding." (Havas dispatch on the 1st)

An Understanding Atmosphere Between France and Germany: An Echo of Hitler's Declaration; French Press Studies Possibility of Negotiations 41

Frankfurt – A report from the press explains the future of Franco-German relations and important discussions promoting understanding between the two countries, saying that a Paris correspondent reported the speech of Mr. Piéllingue, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee. Mr. Piéllingue's speech was based on Hitler's recent important diplomatic and political declaration, stating that if substantial results are desired, the first thing is to not dwell on past grievances. Only by not dwelling on past grievances can the current difficulties be resolved. The Saar vote has completely resolved the land dispute. Chancellor Hitler has repeatedly stated this to the German people and the world. Important figures of the New Germany, such as Hess, Göring, Frick, Goebbels, and Ribbentrop, have also made similar declarations. We have no reason to doubt this guarantee. I personally do not want to delve into their sincerity for a moment, but the principle of recognizing territorial sovereignty should also be applied to French colonies. It is especially appreciated that the German government abides by the Locarno Pact, which guarantees peace in Western Europe. The German people are deeply afraid that invoking the Franco-Soviet Pact signed on May 2 will narrow the scope of the Locarno Pact. The French government will take steps to dispel German unease. Mr. Piéllingue continued, saying that he is well aware of Germany's position regarding the French treaty system. It is not difficult for us to understand that the German government does not want to join a treaty that would inadvertently involve it in war. In short, Germany has no intention of sacrificing a single soldier for such a war. Many French politicians disagree with the current treaty system. I have been one of them since I published my reasons for opposition in the summer of 1934, he said. Mr. Piéllingue believes that the Austrian question is not an insurmountable difficulty, saying that Germany has no right to demand the annexation of Austria. At this point, the correspondent said that the German government only demands that German expatriates in Austria should enjoy the right of self-determination. Mr. Piéllingue admitted that he had no objection to this. Regarding the arms issue, Mr. Piéllingue strongly advocated that both sides should have the freedom to act as they deem appropriate, and said that only strength can command respect, but this does not preclude the possibility of equality in armaments between the two countries. Regarding this matter, France is willing to fairly consider any proposal put forward by Germany. Mr. Piéllingue concluded by saying that Europe used to be in a position to lead the world, but after the war, it was almost reduced to a second-rate position. Like Hitler, I am an optimist and do not believe in the decline of Europe, but in the revival of Europe. To seek the revival of Europe, major powers must cooperate to maintain lasting peace. Regarding this point, France and Germany have a common goal and a vast field for cooperation in the economic sphere, (National Telegram on the 30th)

(Paris) This morning, newspapers are speculating about the possibility of negotiations between France and Germany. Le Journal said that starting negotiations with Germany carries the risk of undermining the Stresa Front. This issue must be considered first. Furthermore, it is impossible to predict what contribution Germany can make to such negotiations. Judging from the situation, it is absolutely impossible for France and Germany to establish an agreement like the Anglo-German agreement. Although Hitler mentioned the issue of disarmament when he attended Congress on May 21, his wording was vague and did not specifically address the issue of Franco-German arms reduction. Moreover, given Germany's current military strength, it is extremely unlikely to establish such an understanding with Germany. Therefore, the newspaper believes that instead of direct Franco-German negotiations, a conference on general European issues should be convened. Even if direct negotiations are desired, opinions should first be exchanged through ordinary diplomatic channels. Le Temps stated that direct negotiations were favored by Briand. German newspapers have said that trust requires courage, which is an irrefutable truth. What we need is to trust ourselves, and then ask for Germany's opinion. If we rely on the British as intermediaries for diplomacy in everything, what good will it do? (National Telegram on the 1st)

Unprecedented Grand Gathering of the Spanish People's Action Party; Agreement Between the Right Wing and the Central Faction; Strong Fortress to Prevent Le Roux's Orders 44

Valencia, Spain – The local Federation of the People's Action Party initiated a grand gathering, with over 125,000 participants. It was presided over by the party leader, Minister of the Army Robles, alongside cabinet members and members of parliament affiliated with the party from various regions. They arrived in 50 train cars, 1,000 buses, and numerous private cars. They gathered at the local national cattle market and football field, where speeches were broadcast via radio. Order at the venue was maintained by members of the party's youth corps, which was excellent. These members all wore uniforms with shirts made of yellow cloth, and saluted by raising their right hands to the left shoulder. Fearing that opposition groups would stage demonstrations and cause disputes, the authorities dispatched security teams carrying machine guns in numerous trucks to patrol everywhere to prevent any accidents. The scale of this gathering was truly rare in Spain. Minister of Communications Roussia delivered a speech, saying, "What Spain needs now are true talents who serve God and the country, not cowardly people. The People's Action Party is not afraid of revolution, but is prepared to stop the left-wing's revolutionary actions to incite the people." Robles then took the stage and said, "The People's Action Party and the Radical Party led by Premier Lerroux have formed an alliance in Salamanca last Sunday." (Note: Lerroux delivered a speech there last Sunday, saying that he would maintain the unity of the government majority, while Robles said that he accepted the republican system with a sincere attitude.) However, although I and Premier Lerroux have signed an alliance, both parties still maintain their original theories and have not abandoned them. In the past, revolutionary tides swept the country, and the Spanish national spirit and material values were in danger of being destroyed. The country was in danger, so we resolutely took on the responsibility of saving the country in order to preserve the foundation of the country. I dare say that the agreement between the People's Action Party and the Radical Party is a strong fortress to prevent revolution." Robles then explained the political program of the right-wing and central factions' group: (1) to do everything possible to eliminate the revolutionary spirit that launched the rebellion in October 1934; (2) to reform the administrative organs and create a clean and frugal government; (3) to reform the constitution. No incidents occurred until the end of the meeting. The venue of this gathering was the same place where former left-wing Republican Prime Minister Azaña gave a speech to over 60,000 people, only a few weeks apart, (Havas Telegram on the 30th)

Instruction from Chairman Chiang: The Current Urgent Tasks of Governing Sichuan and Saving the Nation – Address at the Expanded Memorial Week in Chengdu 74

Chengdu Air News, June 14th, 9:00 AM: The fourth Expanded Memorial Week presided over by Chairman Chiang in Chengdu was held. Attendees included Chairman Chiang, Secretary-General Yang, Director He, Director Kang, Chairman Liu, General Liu, military generals, party and government personnel, and representatives from all sectors of the public, totaling over one thousand people. After Chairman Chiang led the attendees in performing the rituals, Chairman Chiang delivered the following address:

"Chairman Liu, fellow comrades, today we are holding the fourth Memorial Week for the Premier here, and it is also the fourth time I have spoken publicly in Chengdu. Now, I will first reiterate the main points of my previous three speeches, and everyone should seriously reflect on them. The first speech concerned my mission in coming to Sichuan this time, which was not solely to suppress the Red bandits, but to inform the responsible leaders of all sectors in Sichuan about how to invigorate themselves, strengthen themselves, and fulfill their duties in the future. On the one hand, we must enable the people of Sichuan Province to fulfill their individual responsibilities, so that progress can be made day by day in politics, the military, society, and all other aspects. I also specifically offered the five words 'public,' 'sincere,' 'simple,' 'unskillful,' and 'strict' as sincere advice to everyone, taking them as the fundamental ways to uplift people's hearts, change the social atmosphere, govern politics and the military, and build Sichuan to save the nation. The key to whether Sichuan is well-governed or in chaos, and whether the nation survives or perishes, lies entirely in this. Everyone must strive to practice this in order to accomplish our mission and achieve the goals of the revolution. The second speech was to inform the leaders of all sectors that bandit suppression must adhere to the principle of 'three parts military, seven parts politics,' and fully leverage the power of politics. To leverage the power of politics, we must also leverage the power of the people. If everyone can work hard according to this, no matter how strong the Red bandits are, it will not be difficult for us to eliminate them. Therefore, not only should the military love and protect the people and intensify the organization and training of the people wherever they go, but the leaders of all sectors of the people must also shoulder this responsibility even more. The principle of 'using the people is better than using soldiers, teaching the people should be like teaching soldiers' should be applied to bandit suppression, resisting foreign insults, governing the country, and bringing peace to the world. Because the number of people is large and they are everywhere, as long as we organize and train them, we can exert the greatest power, and utilizing them is much more convenient than utilizing the military. However, to use the people, we must first save the people, and training the people must be like training the military, so that they can share life and death and adversity with us, and devote their efforts to the work of bandit suppression and resisting foreign insults. The third speech was to say that the leaders of all sectors individually bear the responsibility of education. Because we want to uplift people's hearts, change the social atmosphere, and enable all citizens in society to cultivate both morality and skills, achieve success, and attain the goals of revolution and national salvation, we must focus on implementing education that combines both literary and military aspects. The education in literary schools should take martial arts as its main foundation, and the education in the military should also take literary matters as its important content, so as to ensure that every citizen becomes a versatile talent who is both literate and martial. Especially martial arts education, which is even more important in today's national crisis. If the people do not understand martial arts, then it is not education for saving the country. Therefore, to be a modern citizen, one must have the cultivation of martial arts. To make education effective, there must be martial arts training. Moreover, martial arts education not only focuses on martial arts, but also needs to cultivate the martial virtues of 'wisdom, trustworthiness, benevolence, courage, and strictness.' As for general education, it should take the 'six arts' as its main content. Only in this way can we achieve holistic education. Only this kind of education can save the country. The words I have spoken in the previous three times are all fundamental ways to suppress bandits, govern Sichuan, and carry out revolution to save the country. They are also the most important principles for you to follow as leaders, officials, and teachers. Everyone, please carefully reflect on whether you have wholeheartedly and earnestly done as I said in the past three weeks. Today, I will continue to talk to you about the key points of educating the people and changing customs, and I hope everyone will pay special attention. Everyone must know what education is. It is a means of teaching people how to be people and how to succeed in their careers. If a country or a society does not have good education, it will not be able to create perfect talents and good customs and cultures, nor will it be able to build a new society and a strong country. Now, if we want to change the social atmosphere, strengthen the people, build a new society, and save the country from danger, we must focus on the education of the people. Besides the combination of literary and military skills that I talked about last time, which should be earnestly put into practice, the leaders of all sectors who are responsible for education, whether literary or military, must understand the entire relationship of national education. The most important thing is to know what the relationship with the people is. Whether we are soldiers or ordinary people, we are the same person. Why is one called a soldier and the other called a civilian? Is it because a person is called a soldier when they wear a military hat, military uniform, and carry a gun, and otherwise they are called a civilian? This is just a slight difference in form. In fact, soldiers and civilians were originally one entity, and there is no absolute difference. Anyone can be a soldier, and any soldier is a civilian. In ancient times in our country, soldiers were embedded in agriculture. When the country was in trouble, everyone had the obligation to be a soldier. When the country was at peace, everyone would return to their fields. It can be seen that soldiers are civilians and civilians are soldiers, and there is no distinction between soldiers and civilians. Since soldiers and civilians are one entity, the education that is given should of course be the same. However, once a person becomes a soldier, the responsibilities they bear are more serious than those of ordinary people. Because their responsibilities are more serious, only citizens with superior moral character and skills can be soldiers. From this, it can be seen that the education of soldiers must be higher than that of ordinary people, and ordinary people are the source of soldiers. That is why I often say that good citizens are the foundation of good soldiers, and good soldiers are the model of good citizens. If a country does not have good people, it will not have good soldiers, and without good soldiers, it will certainly not be able to form a sound army. We must have good people in order to produce a good army. At the same time, because soldiers bear greater responsibilities than ordinary people, their character, intelligence, and the spirit of sacrifice of 'forgetting the family for the country,' 'forgetting the self for the public,' and 'courageously doing what is right' should also be higher than that of ordinary people. Therefore, soldiers should be models for ordinary people. If soldiers and the entire army are really this good, then ordinary people can of course be directly and indirectly influenced by them in tangible and intangible ways, and have the same noble character, perfect intelligence, and spirit of public service as our soldiers, so that they can fight alongside our army and complete the cause of national salvation and rejuvenation. Therefore, if we want to truly train good soldiers and make our country strong, we must first find ways to educate the people of the whole country and make them excellent modern citizens. However, to achieve this quickly, in addition to the leaders of all sectors of the people working hard to train them through educational methods, the military must also take on this responsibility. (To be continued)"

Liu Xiang Announces the Guidelines for the Governance of Sichuan Province 75

Establish New Systems to Gradually Purify Local Administration, Save Money and Ensure Fiscal Balance.

Chongqing Correspondence: The Red bandits on the North and South routes are being pursued and attacked relentlessly by the Central Army and various Sichuan bandit suppression forces. They are increasingly cornered in the barren areas of western Sichuan. Most of the counties they previously occupied have been recovered. The Xu bandits only hold Mao County, Wenchuan, and Liban three counties, while the Zhu Mao bandits only hold Danleng and Lian gong two places. Western Sichuan is poor and materially difficult. The Yi people in the mountains deeply hate the bandits. The bandits are trapped in a large encirclement by government troops and have lost their ability to plunder. They have no chance of survival. The Sichuan Provincial Government has also decided to move to Chengdu at the beginning of next month. Deng Mingjie, Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, recently telegraphed from the province, instructing the Provincial Government to move part of its staff on the 10th of next month. All departments are currently preparing for the move to the west. Chairman Liu of the Provincial Government has recently announced the guidelines for this year's administration and provided explanations, outlining new measures in civil administration, finance, construction, education, and security, which are extremely practical. The following is a record:

"Since the reorganization of the Sichuan Provincial Government, several months have passed in a flash. Although government orders have gradually moved towards unification, there are still many problems to be addressed and shortcomings to be overcome. We are unable to achieve anything due to the difficulty of managing things. Considering the current situation in Sichuan, which has become the focus of national attention, and the expectations of all parties for us, which are far-reaching and significant, although we may not be able to achieve success overnight to meet the urgent needs of the people, we should still overcome all difficulties and work step by step to seek gradual progress. We should make monthly plans and instruct the various departments of the government to formulate guidelines based on their respective duties, the urgent needs of the current situation, and in accordance with laws and regulations, to serve as a fixed schedule for the year. In terms of civil administration, we should first establish political systems to adapt to the new environment, then train talents and implement new laws and regulations. Within a year, we must ensure that the local administrative sector gradually evolves, eliminating the corrupt and chaotic images of the past, so that the people can have a fresh perspective. In terms of finance, we should reorganize finance, establish treasuries, and adhere to the principle of living within our means, with unified revenue and expenditure as a fixed schedule. We should establish a financial reorganization committee to plan and discuss reforms, and implement financial transparency. Within this year, even if we dare not expect to increase revenue quickly, we should do our best to reduce expenditure to achieve financial stability and balance revenue and expenditure. In terms of construction, we should improve agriculture, develop transportation, improve local products, and utilize the power of the people within the scope of our human and financial resources. As for large-scale light and heavy industries, we should start with preparation and investigation and avoid rushing to create a facade to avoid waste and ensure practical results. In terms of education, we should reduce redundant departments, reorganize education funding, enrich school content, establish more vocational schools, and implement cooperation between construction and education to ensure that learning is useful and that what is learned is applied. We should strive to eliminate the empty and scattered malpractices of the past and establish a robust and practical style of learning within this year, improve the bad habits of young people, recover bandit areas, implement special education to correct deteriorated thinking, and cultivate national consciousness to guide students' trends. In terms of security, we should follow the major guidelines for improvement issued by Chairman Chiang, consider the current situation in Sichuan, unify funding, streamline staffing, strictly train, and clear up local group contributions in various counties to ensure that the people have practical self-defense benefits. The above outline is by no means a far-reaching plan. If we can implement it effectively, we will not make any major mistakes. My humble intention is to show sincerity with simplicity rather than using empty talk to buy favor. The reason why I must list the main points and make them public is to encourage mutual restraint and accelerate the self-motivation of my colleagues. I do not want to rigidly adhere to small achievements and be complacent. As the saying goes, 'A high platform rises from accumulated earth, and a journey of a hundred miles begins with a single step.' The items listed above are like a drop in the ocean. In terms of the future of politics, it is far away. Since I have served my hometown for many years, I have drifted with the tide and wasted years, failing to make active contributions to benefit my homeland. Now, I have encountered an opportunity to reverse the situation, and I dare not be slack or miss this opportunity. Regardless of whether we should start with reforming politics to transform Sichuan, even if we are only dedicated to completing the bandit suppression work, it will not succeed without exerting the function of politics and military affairs in parallel. However, I am aware of my own limited abilities and may not be able to reverse the situation, but my determination to fill the sea with earth has not changed. My sincere heart should be understood by all. I hope that all my elders and brothers in Sichuan will uphold the spirit of mutual concern and advance hand in hand with sincerity, making progress day by day and working diligently to achieve success, so that what I say today will all be put into practice within a year, which will be the shared glory of our homeland. In addition to submitting special reports to the central government, I will summarize the purpose of formulating the implementation guidelines for the provincial government this year for the reference of all my fellow villagers. Liu Xiang, Chairman of the Sichuan Provincial Government."

River Water Continues to Rise: Hanyang Embankment Collapses: Entire Seventy Li of Hancheng Embankment Collapses, Flooding Thousands of Acres of Land: Several Breaches in Huangpi Minsheng Embankment, Also in Imminent Danger 76

Hankou Communication: The river water is rising rapidly day by day, and the situation is tense. The people of Wuhan are trembling with fear. The great flood of twenty years ago caused great pain, leading to a change in the color of the water. The dikes in Wuhan are generally solid, but some projects are poorly built and difficult to guarantee, which is unavoidable. Yesterday, outside the Zhanggong Dike, the Hancheng Embankment in Hanyang, which stretches for more than seventy li, completely collapsed in the heavy rain, flooding more than ten thousand acres of land. This is the first dike collapse of the year. The founder of the embankment was Li Jiehou, a local gentry. He did not make precise plans in advance. The estimated cost of the project was 200,000 yuan, which was submitted to the Construction Department for approval, and the county magistrate was assigned to be responsible for supervising the construction. It was stipulated that part of the funds would be raised locally, and part would be advanced by the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee. However, after construction began, there were no funds to raise locally, so the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee took on the task alone. Because the amount borrowed exceeded the agreed amount, supply could not meet demand, and all projects could not proceed according to the procedures, stopping and starting intermittently. From last year to this spring, only half of the project was completed. After the peach blossoms flooded, the water level gradually rose, and the officials and gentry responsible for supervising the construction began to panic. They decided to conscript laborers to speed up the construction in the hope of completing it as soon as possible. However, the procedures for conscripting laborers were extremely cumbersome. In the middle of this month, sixty to seventy people were conscripted, and they worked for several days until the continuous heavy rain. On the 21st, a section of Tajiatou first reported a collapse, and another section collapsed on the 23rd. Yesterday, it completely collapsed and could not be saved. More than ten thousand acres of farmland were flooded, and the construction cost of more than 200,000 yuan was completely washed away. In addition, the Minsheng Embankment, located outside the Zhanggong Dike in Huangpi County, has been under construction for seven or eight years. Several breaches have now occurred, and the situation is precarious. If the water level rises further, it may also collapse. (30th)

Songjiang: Drowning Death Due to Lack of Swimming Skills 77

Gu Zhiming, a former police officer, was originally from Huaian, where he farmed for a living. Unaccustomed to public service, he resigned and moved his family to a village about three li south of Lita Hui Town in this county, where he rented land to farm, returning to his old occupation. His son studied barbering. His son's name was Baojun, and he was nineteen years old. He currently works in a tea house owned by the Zhu family in the town, which is enough to make a living. Recently, due to the hot weather, Jiang Peigen and Shen Achuan from the Tianyitang pharmacy invited Baojun to bathe in the Changshan River. The river was newly completed. Gu had no knowledge of swimming. Once he entered the water, he was panting, sweating, and physically exhausted. When he reached the center of the river, he tragically drowned. Companions Jiang and Shen, seeing that disaster had struck, returned without regard for him. Gu Zhiming was very saddened upon hearing the report and reported it to the nearby public security branch. Jiang Peigen and Shen Achuan were summoned to the bureau. After preliminary interrogation, they have been transferred to the local court for review. It is reported that Gu Baojun's body has not yet been retrieved.

Public Security Bureau Chief He Runzhang, due to repeated theft cases in the city, cooperated with the Chief Inspector, patrolling officers, and special agents to patrol all night in groups. Since the implementation, thieves have been caught many times. One day at 6:00 p.m., he personally led Chief Inspector He, patrolling officer Lu, and others to patrol outside the South Gate and apprehended three suspicious persons wearing military uniforms with symbols. According to the interrogation, they were smuggling salt, named Zhang Shijian, Gao Fugui, and Huang Zhanyuan. However, the three people's statements differed, so they were taken to the bureau for detention pending investigation.

Suzhou: Three-Level, Three-Trial System Implemented 79

All levels of courts in Jiangsu Province have been ordered to implement a three-level, three-trial system from July 1st. The summary courts and collegial panels of each court will be abolished. In the future, second-instance cases will be handled by the High Court. The Chief Prosecutor must personally investigate the cases. The number of appealed cases to the High Court will inevitably increase, and it is planned to establish a third civil court. However, due to personnel selection and procedural issues, it has not been possible to implement this yet. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Justice and Administration for approval. It is also reported that from the 1st, the office hours of each court will be changed to 7:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m.

More than 10,000 mu of lake land in East Taihu Lake have been enclosed by guest residents. Yangzhou: Liuyu River Bank Collapses Again 81

The situation of the Liuyu River bank being repeatedly eroded by the river waves recently, it is now known that the river mouth on the 30th, due to the extremely strong southwest wind, the river flow along the Zhenjiang car ferry terminal area was unusually rapid. At 4:30 p.m., when the sixth downstream car arrived at the South Station, the flow was even more rapid. The newly padded wharf in front of the pontoon boat showed cracks again. When the ferry arrived at the port, the flow was too strong and the vortex too deep. After several twists and turns, it was able to dock on the shore. By the time of the last train, the flow was slightly smaller. At the east end of the dock neck, another corner is about to collapse (a corner has already collapsed). If this corner can be collapsed together, it would be safer. The car company is currently trying to maintain it and plans to install another row of piles to temporarily ensure safety.

Soldier of the 83rd Division Stabbed to Death by a Taiwanese 86

The Murderer Has Been Handed Over to the Japanese Consulate for Legal Action

(Fuzhou) On the 30th of this month, Qiu Chao-shui, a Taiwanese on Xiatin Fanjiang Houlu in this city, stabbed to death Zhang Jinhe, a soldier of the 494th Regiment of the 83rd Division stationed at the Provincial Office. Zhang and his colleague Ye Dexiang took monkeys to Yunzhang Road on the morning of the 30th. Unexpectedly, the monkey's paw suddenly grabbed the corner of Taiwanese Qiu Chao-yong's clothes. Zhang Jinhe immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Qiu saw that the situation was not good and fled into Zhenli Foreign Firm. Qi Dexiang saw that Zhang Jinhe was seriously injured and ran to report to the police, and reported to the office. Knowing the whereabouts of the murderer, he notified the port police department by telephone. At the same time, he led the team to monitor the vicinity of Zhenhe Foreign Firm with police officers. Japanese Police Chief Liu Dehe led several Japanese police officers to arrive. The Japanese police entered the building to search. The murderer Qiu Chao-yong jumped down from the upper floor and was arrested by the Japanese police. Qiu's clothes and pants still had blood stains. He was interrogated in the company. He confessed that he was 24 years old, from 33 Yutian-cho 2-chome, Keelung City, Taiwan. He arrived in Xiamen on the Fengshan Maru on March 7 this year, and arrived in Fuzhou on the Hai Ning Maru from Xiamen on April 1, staying in Zhao Chang Foreign Firm or Man Tai Foreign Firm. Because the deceased's monkey grabbed my clothes, I had an argument with him. I took a pig knife from Zhao Chang Foreign Firm and stabbed the deceased in the back, causing his death. After the interrogation, the Japanese Police Chief took the murderer back to the Japanese Consulate for interrogation in accordance with the law. (1st Central News Agency telegram)

Key Points of the Outline for the Management of Sugar Transportation and Sales 87

(Nanjing) The main points of the fourteen-article outline for the management of sugar transportation and sales are announced. Sugar for transportation and sales refers to refined sugar, crude sugar, syrup, and sucrose containing 50% or more. The Management Committee may entrust a Chinese-national sugar company jointly run by officials and merchants to handle sugar purchase and sale affairs. The sugar company may entrust legitimate sugar merchants in major commercial ports and various places as sales managers to operate the sugar transportation and sales business in their respective areas. The sugar purchased by the sugar company should be stored in customs warehouses or designated bonded warehouses, and may not be withdrawn without paying national tax. When purchasing foreign sugar, the sugar company should purchase it according to the world's lowest market price and the principle of competitive bidding. All domestic sugar material planters and sugar manufacturers should register the type and quantity with the Management Committee. Sugar merchants in various places who sell sugar may, if necessary, petition the Management Committee to request the Ministry of Finance and local authorities to assist in the search for smuggled sugar. If any are seized, bonuses will be given according to a percentage. (1st special telegram)

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Explains Ambiguities in Organizing Farmers' Associations 94

As for areas where farmers' associations have not been established, according to Article 13 of the Farmers' Association Law, township farmers' associations should be initiated automatically by members in the area, and higher-level farmers' associations have no right to add them on their behalf. Reuters Special Commercial Report, July 1st 113

Gold and Silver

London gold price today is one hundred and forty-one shillings and four and a half pence, the same as the price on Saturday and Sunday.

London silver market is stable today. Spot price is thirty-one and twenty-five pence, and futures are thirty-one and a half pence, both unchanged. India and speculators bought in, and China sold out.

Mount Lyell Silver: The silver futures market was closed today, so there is no report.

Exchange Rate

British and American: There was little excitement in the London foreign exchange market today, and the exchange rate hardly changed. The closing price of the US and British was the same. It rose three one two five in the first hour, the noon price did not move, and then fell three one two five. In the afternoon, it rose to four yuan, nine jiao, four fen, three one two five, which was one eight seven five higher than the opening.

British and French: The opening price was 74 francs, 46, which was four pounds lower than the opening on Sunday. It rose a pound in the first hour, unchanged at noon, and then fell four pounds, becoming 74 francs, 47. This price did not change until 2 pm, rising one pound from the opening.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening price fell today, with the July price falling one pound to 11.82, but then it fell five pounds to 11.77. Later, the price had a slight upward trend. The weather in the cotton belt is uncertain, and there is no need for much rain everywhere.

Chicago Wheat: It was light today, and the price was almost unchanged from the last closing. Later, the price of wheat and miscellaneous grains all rose due to poor weather reports and few consumer stocks. The weather in the grain belt is uncertain, and there is no need for much rain. The weather in other production areas in the southwest is sunny and hot, but the barometer reading is quite low. There are many thunderstorms in the northwest, which can make morning crops wither. The forecast is for the weather to turn cold and unstable.

Liverpool Cotton: Still stable today, with the July price at 6.45 at 1 pm, down one pound.

New York was more stable today, with the opening rising five pounds. There was a stable phenomenon in the morning. The opening price was able to remain unchanged, and trading was slightly sluggish.

The Public Assembly is scheduled to vote on this case today. The market situation was still stable in the morning. Oil stocks and steel stocks rose slightly, but in general, trading was quite sluggish. The average price of Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks was 118.26, up five pounds. Local News

Shanghai City: Compulsory Literacy Education Began Yesterday, Over 60,000 Illiterates Enthusiastically Enrolled 114

Shanghai News Agency reported that the compulsory literacy education in this city has been implemented since yesterday. The first phase of 220 municipal literacy schools have all opened separately. The Literacy Education Committee has an inspection plan, and the mayor has also organized a secret investigation team to visit various schools to inspect the teaching situation at any time. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

The First Phase of Literacy Schools Opened Yesterday

Except for the three districts of Luxing, Gaoxing, and Zhenru, which are purely rural areas and inconvenient to open schools during the busy season, the remaining 19 districts have established schools according to the situation in each district, ranging from two to thirty schools, totaling 220 schools, all of which opened simultaneously yesterday and held simple ceremonies separately. The directors and teachers of each school reported. Yesterday, the reporter visited the literacy schools in the two urban areas of South Shanghai and Zhabei. The principals of each school borrowed temples, ancestral halls, public offices, schools, institutions, and groups, etc. The school names were all called Shanghai Municipal XX Road Literacy School, with white characters on a black background, inscribed by Mayor Wu. The people who were required to enroll all enrolled enthusiastically without fear. Although the clothing was not uniform, it was still neat. Most of them were coolies, and they were also polite to the teachers and had a strong interest. Tao, the director-general of the association, visited various schools and was very satisfied.

Strictly Established Inspection Methods

In order to assess and supervise the diligence of teachers in the literacy schools in each district, and to provide guidance at any time, the Literacy Education Committee has assigned four inspectors to rotate to visit. Mayor Wu also compiled a secret investigation team among the civil servants to secretly assign them to various districts for investigation. In addition, the offices in each district formed an academic affairs committee with enthusiastic educators to be responsible for supervision. The literacy schools will still have classes on Sundays and will not have holidays. The Literacy Education Committee has specially stipulated substitute teaching methods. Every ten schools (that is, ten teachers) will have one substitute teacher, who will substitute for each teacher for two days each month, so that the teachers in each school can rest for two days each month. The district offices will propose four substitute teachers, and the Literacy Education Committee will select one of them for employment. In addition to substituting for 20 days each month, the substitute teachers will also be responsible for inspection, so the supervision of each school has been very strict.

The Municipal Government Awards School Supplies

The students' school supplies are a Big Leather pencil and a paper notebook, totaling four cents, which students should purchase from the school. However, if the family is poor and never absent from class, or the absence does not exceed one-sixth, and the grades are above B, they will all be awarded by the municipal government. It is heard that the municipal government has prepared 200,000 copies, and the textbooks for students will all be given away and will not be charged.

Key Points of the Sino-French Vietnam Commercial Treaty: Overseas Chinese Can Freely Enter and Exit Vietnam, and the Head Tax on Overseas Chinese is Reduced by Half 120

New Voice News Agency reported that after the expiration of the Sino-French Vietnam Commercial Treaty, the Vietnamese authorities wantonly destroyed the commercial activities of overseas Chinese and the import of Chinese goods because there was no treaty relationship. Our country believed that the Vietnamese side did not adhere to the spirit of reciprocity for the import of French goods, so it could not be given the same treatment as in the past. Therefore, both sides have suffered adverse effects in commerce. Recently, the French side, through the French ambassador to China and our central diplomatic authorities, proceeded to renew the commercial treaty, and the issue of renewing the Vietnam commercial treaty, which had been in progress for several years and had not been resolved, was resolved. Many of our overseas Chinese are engaged in business in Vietnam, and the commercial transactions are also very frequent. The conclusion of this commercial treaty is quite convenient for the people of both sides. The most important points are recorded below: Our country will levy an import tax on Vietnamese rice, stipulating that each 100 kilograms will be subject to a customs duty of 1.5 yuan, which is a reduction of half a corner compared to the current tax rate. Vietnamese coal imports are stipulated to be subject to a tax of 9 mills and a half per ton, while the current tax regulations levy 2.8 yuan. As for the import tax on Chinese goods levied by Vietnam, it will generally be levied according to the tax rate set in 1910. Goods passing through Vietnam from Yunnan will be subject to a transit tax of 25%, which is now reduced to 1%. In addition, the head tax on overseas Chinese levied by the Annam government will also be reduced by half according to the current amount. The establishment of additional consulates has also been resolved. When the commercial treaty is implemented, our country will set up consulates in Saigon, Hanoi, Haiphong, and other places, and Chinese can also enter the country freely.

Central News Agency reported that Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, had a sharp increase in body temperature from June 28th. However, according to Dr. Noël's opinion, President Wang must undergo strict recuperation for a longer period of time, otherwise it will be quite dangerous. Therefore, President Wang decided to stay in the hospital for treatment. It is not certain when he will return to Beijing. The affairs of the Executive Yuan will be temporarily handled by Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance. Postal Savings and Remittance Bureaus Were Merged Yesterday: Shen Shuyu Was Reappointed as Deputy Director of the Postal Administration 122

Central News Agency reported that the Central Government decided to merge the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau with the Postal Administration. It was officially implemented yesterday. Wang Zhijing, the director of the secretariat of the bureau, who was sent to the central government for instructions, returned to Shanghai by night train the day before yesterday and reported to Director Shen at the bureau yesterday about the situation of the negotiations in Beijing. According to Wang, the reporter of the Central News Agency stated that the bureau will be renamed the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau from July 1st. The central government will issue a separate seal, which will be received soon. Director Shen Shuyu took office as Deputy Director of the Postal Administration on the same day. All bureau staff will be reappointed separately. In the future, except for the accounting department, which will remain independent, the administrative part will be under the Postal Administration. As for the local postal savings and remittance bureaus, they will also be renamed sub-bureaus.

Sugar Committee Actively Working to Ban Private Sugar and Impose Heavy Taxes for Revenue and Hygiene; Rumors of Monopoly are Absolutely False 123

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the Ministry of Finance recently approved fourteen articles of the "Outline for the Management of Sugar Transportation and Sales," the full text of which has been published in various newspapers. However, some Chinese and foreign sugar merchants in Shanghai still seem unclear about the establishment of the Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee by the Ministry of Finance. There has been much speculation, with some saying it is a practice of monopoly, or a preliminary step towards monopoly. There are also doubts about the soon-to-be-established China Sugar Company. Among the 64 members of the Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, 38 have jointly published a statement declaring that they have not joined the company. It is also heard that foreign sugar merchants are mostly taking a wait-and-see attitude, and opinions vary. In order to understand the content, the reporter of the Shenshi News Agency specifically visited the committee yesterday. According to Mr. Chen, the section chief of the committee, the purpose of establishing the Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee by the Ministry of Finance is to eliminate private sugar, promote domestic production, safeguard tax revenue, replenish the national treasury, and regulate sugar prices, in order to eliminate merchant speculation. The investigation of the production and sales of sugar is to prevent tax evasion, balance market prices, and ensure that sugar is not adulterated with other sugar substances, in order to prioritize public health. The reporter further asked about the rumored intention of the government to monopolize sugar by establishing a sugar company. Mr. Chen stated that there was absolutely no such intention. Sugar monopoly has no legal basis, which is well known. Moreover, according to Article 6 of the Outline, the sugar company should purchase sugar at the lowest possible market price, and Article 7 stipulates that the sugar company shall not arbitrarily raise prices to seek speculative profits when promoting sales, so as to avoid the abuses of monopoly. Therefore, all sugar merchants can trade freely with the sugar company, without any conflict. Legitimate merchants will not only not be affected by the establishment of the sugar company, but will also indirectly benefit from it, because adulterated sugar containing saccharin and other powdered substances, as well as tax-evading private sugar, must be prohibited from sale, which will inevitably increase the business of legitimate merchants. On the part of the sugar company, there are clear provisions in the Outline and it is governed by economic principles, so there will be no bias in transportation and sales. Moreover, the sugar company will set up sales offices and distribution points, and each place that sells sugar will enjoy commissions. The more sales, the more commissions, so everyone will be happy to refuse to sell private sugar. If there is smuggling, the officials can be notified to carry out crackdowns. In this way, there will be benefits to government tax revenue. As for foreign sugar merchants, if they are unwilling to violate China's tax laws and seek the development of their business through legitimate channels, they will be welcomed to cooperate with the China Sugar Company. In short, the establishment of the Sugar Management Committee by the Ministry of Finance is actually in a guiding and assisting position for the legitimate business of Chinese and foreign sugar merchants, with only benefits and no harm. Currently, the work of the committee is actively underway. Mr. Chen said that the China Sugar Company is a commercial organization, and if it does not violate the current laws and regulations of the country, the government cannot interfere with its scheduled establishment.

Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance Borrows 300,000 Yuan in Shanghai; Two Banks Have Already Delivered the Funds 124

According to the World News Agency, the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance recently borrowed 300,000 yuan from the Agricultural Bank of China and the Central Bank to repay the principal and interest of public bonds. According to banking circles, the loan was undertaken by the Agricultural Bank of China for 200,000 yuan, secured by the tax revenue from foil production in Zhejiang Province, and by the Central Bank for 100,000 yuan, secured by the salt surtax revenue, at a monthly interest rate of 1%. Because Zhejiang Province needs to repay the principal and interest of three types of public bonds, including disaster relief, old debt clearance, and highway construction, by the end of June, in addition to the more than 300,000 yuan held by the Public Debt Fund Management Committee, there is still a shortfall of about 300,000 yuan, so the loan was taken from the two banks to cover the payment. The agreement was signed and delivered on the 30th of last month, and transferred to the Hangzhou branch of the Bank of China and the Zhejiang Local Bank for disbursement of the principal and interest of the public bonds.

China National Aviation Corporation Resumes Chongqing-Kunming Route; Scheduled to Fly from Chongqing to Kunming on the 5th of this Month 125

The Chongqing-Kunming route of the China National Aviation Corporation, which passes through Guiyang from Chongqing to Kunming, is located in the most inconvenient area of transportation in the west. Since the company was ordered by the Ministry of Communications to actively prepare, the equipment was completed in March of this month, and the first flight was made on the 25th of that month using a Ford aircraft. Afterwards, it traveled between Chongqing and Guiyang, but has not yet officially opened to Kunming. According to reliable sources, the new Ford aircraft purchased by the company was flown to Shanghai for repairs a few days ago. Now, the three engines of the aircraft have been installed and will fly back to Chongqing on the 2nd. The official flight from Chongqing to Kunming is scheduled to start on July 5th, and will then fly according to the original schedule.

River Water Rises Sharply; Steamboats Limited in Speed 126

Recently, the weather has been continuously阴雨, and the water levels of the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have risen sharply, causing increasing obstacles for steamboats. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received telegrams from various ports along the Yangtze River, stating that the water level of the Han River had exceeded 43 feet above the water mark, and the river water along the banks had already submerged the embankment feet, and low-lying areas had reached the embankment. The Wuhan Flood Control Association is carrying out protection work at various points along the embankment. Various shipping companies are also preparing flood prevention work at various wharves and warehouses. Telegrams from Jiujiang and Wuhu both stated that the river water had already flooded the low-lying land of various wharves along the river yesterday, with the water level equal to the shore. If it rises further, the city will also be submerged, and railway bridges will be damaged. All steamboats going up and down the river have been ordered to limit their speed to prevent damage to the embankments.

Xin Feng Collides with a Boat and Runs Aground; Tugboat Damaged Wheelhouse, Suspended Service for Dockyard Repair 127

The Northern Line steamboat "Xin Feng" of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which sailed from Tianjin to Shanghai this time, collided with a tugboat and ran aground en route. It arrived in Shanghai yesterday, and has suspended service for repairs due to damage to the hull. The situation is described below:

Collision in Tianjin: The "Xin Feng" is an older ship, having been in service for forty-four years. This time, it loaded goods and passengers at the Zizhulin Wharf in Tianjin and sailed to Shanghai. When the ship's crew raised anchor and turned the ship's hull, it collided with a tugboat parked there, damaging the wheelhouse. The "Xin Feng" also suffered minor damage.

Grounded and Damaged: The ship sailed from Tianjin. The weather was unfavorable, with continuous heavy rain and persistent fog on the sea. On Sunday, when sailing to the Yawo Sand sea area, it ran aground on Yawo Sand due to fog and low tide, causing minor damage to the bottom of the ship. It was not until the tide rose that the ship's captain, Gao Fa, drove the ship away from the shoal and back to Shanghai.

Suspension of Service for Repairs: The "Xin Feng" arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and berthed at the Jinliyuan Wharf to unload the cargo. The captain reported the collision and grounding to the company. Due to the damage to the hull, the company decided yesterday to suspend the "Xin Feng" from the Northern Line service and immediately send it to the Jiangnan Shipyard for major repairs. The company has issued a letter to notify the insurance company.

According to the Central News Agency, after the Shanghai Municipal Government appointed Wang Xiaolai and others as members of the Anti-Smoking Committee, the committee members held an inauguration ceremony at the Municipal Government yesterday morning, and then held the first meeting, officially starting work from today. The speaker will follow behind the gentlemen and do his best to implement the policy, in order to fully implement the anti-smoking policy.

First Meeting: After the oath of office, the first meeting was held immediately. First, Chairman Wang Xiaolai read out the organizational regulations, and then began the discussion, resolving: (1) the election of standing committee members, and it was resolved to elect Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, and Yan Fuqing as standing committee members; (2) regarding the selection of personnel for the committee, it was resolved that the standing committee members should contact the municipal government for handling; (3) the decision on the office address of the committee, and it was resolved to set the address at 51 Maojia Lane, Nanshi; (4) the date of the committee's meetings, and it was resolved to hold meetings every Monday afternoon at 3:00 PM, with the standing committee members taking turns as chairman.

Office Work Begins Today: The committee will start working at Maojia Lane from today. All staff will be temporarily borrowed from the Municipal Government staff, and it was decided to hold the second meeting next Monday afternoon at 3:00 PM.

The Shanghai Assets of the Eastern Railway Were Received by the Japanese Side Yesterday 129

Entrusted to the International Transportation Company

But the company has not yet officially acknowledged it

According to the World News Agency, the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has formally stated that it does not recognize the illegal sale and purchase of the China Eastern Railway, which is jointly owned by China and Russia, by Japan and Russia as a fait accompli. It is now known that after the sale of the railway by both parties, it has been entrusted by Japan to the South Manchuria Railway Company for management. At that time, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs also stated that the assets of the China Eastern Railway in Shanghai (referring to the China Eastern Railway Business Office and the Yangjiadu Wharf in Pudong) were also included in the sales contract. However, for several days, the receipt of these assets has not been implemented. The Soviet Russian representative is still managing it in Shanghai. It was not until last week that the Japanese and Russian sides secretly began the process of receiving the above two institutions. The Japanese side was entrusted by the Shanghai Office of the South Manchuria Railway Company to the Japan International Transportation Company for handling. It was heard yesterday that the Yangjiadu Wharf in Pudong has already been completely received and started operating yesterday. The China Eastern Railway Business Office at 33 Sichuan Road was also received yesterday and is currently being reorganized. It is expected to start operating today or tomorrow. The reporter met with Mr. Nakano, the general manager of the International Transportation Company, who did not admit to receiving the assets of the China Eastern Railway, saying that it was because the company's original building was too dark, so it moved to 33 Sichuan Road to work. However, other Japanese people in the company all admitted that they had just received it from the Eastern Railway Business Office and were scheduled to start operating today. At the same time, the reporter went to 68 Guangdong Road to investigate the International Transportation Company, but did not see the company preparing to move. The Chinese Enterprise Bank (the landlord of the China Eastern Railway Business Office) also did not see the China Eastern Railway Business Office退租退租 and the International Transportation Company转租转租. All parties have proved that the International Transportation Company has already represented the South Manchuria Railway Company authorities in taking over the Shanghai assets of the China Eastern Railway. It is not yet certain what name will be used to operate the above two institutions in the future. It is generally operated under the name of the International Transportation Company. In addition, the reporter also inquired about this news with the Qingli Office of the Sino-Russian Daosheng Bank, which has a great interest in the issue and once submitted a request to the local court to execute the attachment of the above assets. According to Mr. Yevadensky, the Russian consultant of the bank, they still did not know about it, even if they knew it, they could not do anything about it. As for the lawsuit at the International Court of Justice in The Hague, this is about the entire debt issue between the China Eastern Railway and Daosheng Bank, not just this part of the assets. They will contact the Daosheng Bank Qingli Office in Paris and London to jointly proceed.

Summary of Liyang Spring Relief Efforts 141

The China Relief Society, in conjunction with the Drought Relief Associations of various provinces, the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee, the Liyang Early Disaster Relief Association, and various charitable organizations, carried out spring relief efforts in Liyang, Jiangsu Province. Mr. Li Yunmen was again publicly elected as the director, accompanied by more than ten relief workers, and departed on April 9 to investigate. Reports of the disastrous situation have been previously recorded in the newspaper. According to a report from Director Li Yunmen, he was dispatched to Liyang to handle spring relief in districts 1, 2, 3, 6, and 4, and received 5,050 bags of relief rice and 30,000 yuan in relief funds, as well as 6,000 yuan from the Liyang Drought Relief Association, which were all received successively. The number of relief funds and rice distributed in Liyang districts 1, 2, 3, 6, and 4 are reported separately. In Liyang District 1, 3,633 one-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 363.3 shi of rice distributed; 6,752 two-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 1,350 shi and 0.4 dou of rice distributed; 1,784 three-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 535.2 shi of rice distributed. In total, 12,169 rice tickets were collected, totaling 2,348.9 shi of rice distributed. In District 2, 3,870 one-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 387 shi of rice distributed; 3,931 two-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 786.2 shi of rice distributed; 2,174 three-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 652.2 shi of rice distributed. In total, 9,975 rice tickets were collected, totaling 1,825.4 shi of rice distributed. In District 6, 1,472 two-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 294.4 shi of rice distributed; 3,577 three-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 1,073.1 shi of rice distributed; 1,413 four-dou rice tickets were collected, totaling 565.2 shi of rice distributed. In total, 6,462 rice tickets were collected, totaling 1,912.7 shi of rice distributed. In total, districts 1, 2, 6, and 3 collected 28,606 rice tickets, one ticket per household, totaling 6,007 shi of rice distributed, including 125 shi of rice purchased in Liyang. In District 3, which distributed relief funds, 3,429 two-yuan relief tickets were collected, totaling 6,858 yuan distributed; 4,112 four-yuan relief tickets were collected, totaling 16,448 yuan distributed; 1,700 five-yuan relief tickets were collected, totaling 8,500 yuan distributed; 542 six-yuan relief tickets were collected, totaling 3,252 yuan distributed. In total, 9,783 relief tickets were collected, one ticket per household, totaling 35,058 yuan distributed. During the distribution, the Liyang County Magistrate and various legal organizations were present to supervise. Mr. Xu Picheng, dispatched by Mr. Zhang Zongdu of the Wuxi Tianquan Hall, assisted in everything. The distribution is now complete. Excluding relief expenses, a total of 6,007 shi of relief rice were distributed in Liyang. The Committee transported 5,050 heavy bags of relief rice from Shanghai. In addition to the 4,902 bags distributed, the remaining 148 bags of relief rice were allocated: 110 bags to the Liyang Drought Relief Association, 30 bags to the Liyang Relief Institute, and 8 bags to Beiguzhen in Liyang District 1, which were received by various charitable organizations, providing relief to extremely distressed disaster victims. Relief silver totaling 35,058 yuan and 6,007 shi of rice were distributed. According to districts 1, 2, 6, and 3, there were a total of 28,606 households, and in District 3, there were 9,783 households, totaling over 38,000 disaster-stricken households in districts 1, 2, 3, 4, and 6. Assuming an average of four people per household, the population is over 150,000. Due to the widespread disaster and limited funds, the relief was meager. It is hoped that the autumn harvest will be promising, so that the tragic disaster will not be repeated.

Court Issues Public Notice for Expedited Execution of Civil Cases 142

The Shanghai First Special District Court of Jiangsu issued Public Notice No. 12 yesterday, stating that the number of civil execution cases in the court is increasing daily. To expedite the handling, additional execution clerks have been assigned to handle compulsory execution separately. In accordance with Article 11 of the revised civil execution regulations, the execution office will generally not summon parties unless necessary. In the future, in addition to cases that the court deems should be executed ex officio, parties applying for execution should clearly state the object of execution and appropriate methods of execution in their application, so that the court can verify them without the need for preliminary summons, to avoid delays. This notice is hereby issued for the information of all parties concerned. This notice is issued on July 1, 1935, by Guo Yunguan, President of the Court.

North Shanghai Station Implements New Ticketing System for Rickshaws 143

Starting today, a new system will be implemented at the North Shanghai Station where passengers purchase tickets for rickshaws entering the station to pick up passengers. This measure sweeps away the long-standing problem of rickshaw pullers privately extorting passengers, which passengers generally praise as convenient. The details are explored below. The measures implemented at the station this time are the result of a year of research and rectification of rickshaws entering the station by the two-route transportation department. The measures have been contracted to the Samsung Rickshaw Company. The rickshaw fare is marked on a Shanghai map, with the North Shanghai Station as the center, divided into red and blue circles. For each circle beyond the red line, the fare increases by one dime; for each circle beyond the blue line, the fare increases by two cents, all calculated in silver dollars. The table is printed at the rickshaw ticket window on the east corridor of the North Shanghai Station, which is very easy for passengers to check. The set fare is roughly equal to the ordinary fare, and it is consistent regardless of weather, including the cost for the rickshaw puller to carry the passenger's luggage to the door of the destination, and the rickshaw puller is not allowed to demand any extra money. Before boarding, passengers can purchase tickets in advance at the price. The ticket is in two parts, one part is torn off and given to the rickshaw puller upon arrival, and the other part is kept by the passenger for inquiries about illegal behavior by the rickshaw puller with the railway authorities. The rickshaw pullers all wear uniforms custom-made by the railway authorities for easy identification. It is reported that in order to take care of the livelihood of the rickshaw pullers who originally had licenses to operate at the station, the railway authorities still allow these rickshaw pullers to obtain free licenses to drop off passengers, but they must sign a guarantee with the contractor, Samsung Rickshaw Company, and comply with the regulations and uniform fares stipulated by the railway authorities.

Eurasia Company Implements Short-Range Group Tour Flights Yesterday 144

Time Limited to 12 Minutes Each Time, Limited to 6 Passengers, Fee 10 Yuan

In order to utilize aircraft aviation time and develop its business, the local Eurasia Aviation Company has launched short-range group sightseeing flights, stipulating that each flight will carry six passengers, with a fee of ten yuan per person and a time limit of 12 minutes per flight. The company has also drafted nine measures, which officially came into effect yesterday. According to Mr. Zha Zhenhu, Secretary of the Company, to an reporter from the Industrial Society, the sightseeing flights are not limited to a specific date. Flights will take off as soon as six passengers are assembled. If the time needs to be extended, an additional sixty yuan will be charged for every fifteen minutes, but the maximum time shall not exceed two hours. Tourists must first purchase tickets directly from the company's business department, and then a car will be sent to pick them up. The sightseeing area of the Shanghai station is limited to the entire city of Shanghai, and other branch stations such as Nanjing, Hankou, Beiping, and Guangzhou will also hold flights at the same time.

U.S. Court Prohibits Raven from Leaving Shanghai 147

Raven had not yet submitted the surety bond yesterday afternoon, reports the North-China Daily News. Mr. He Fu, Liquidator of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation, filed a lawsuit with the U.S. Court for China last Saturday (June 29), ordering Raven, former General Manager of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation, American Eastern Banking Company, Pui Yee Land Company, and Pui Yee Bank, to immediately return silver 135,000 taels. Mr. He Fu told people yesterday (Sunday) that his lawsuit against Raven was intended to recover this 135,000 taels for the creditors. Mr. He Fu also applied to the U.S. Court before midnight on Saturday to issue an order preventing Raven from leaving China, as it was heard that Raven was trying to hastily leave the Republic of China and escape the jurisdiction of the U.S. Court. Chief Judge Helmick of the U.S. Court approved the application and ordered Raven to post a bond of US$20,000.

It was learned from U.S. Court bailiff Fuber at 6 p.m. on Sunday that Raven had not yet deposited the bond with the court. However, Mr. Fu claimed that since today was Sunday, it would naturally be difficult for Raven to raise the required bond. He decided to give Raven the opportunity to deposit it on Monday, so he did not take immediate severe action. Deputy bailiff Peterson will be residing at Raven's residence at 555 Hongqiao Road tonight. It is noted that on January 13, 1932, the board of directors of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation passed the following resolution:

"Because Raven, General Manager, Manager and Initiator of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation, has served for a long time, and has been loyal and sincere, and has never taken a salary or other compensation, it is resolved to grant him an honorarium of 135,000 taels to reward his loyal service, and it is resolved to order the treasurer to pay Raven all of this amount, and to write off this amount from the company's books within six years or less. In 1932, 35,000 taels should be written off, and the remaining amount should be written off in any year depending on the amount of net profit earned by the company during this period."

According to Mr. He Fu's interview with a newspaper reporter, judging from the wording of the resolution, the contents of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation at that time were already empty. We must pay attention to the fact that 135,000 taels were immediately paid to Raven, and that the amount was written off from the bank's books in six years, and that the bank did not owe Raven a single cent at that time. All of this is sufficient to prove that the contents of the bank were already empty at that time, and he believes that Raven must have known this situation well. Mr. He Fu also said that when the board of directors of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation passed a resolution to grant Raven 135,000 taels in cash, the American Eastern Banking Company and the Pui Yee Land Company also paid Raven the same amount of gratuity. In the near future, the American Eastern Banking Company and the Pui Yee Land Company will also sue Raven for this reason. One more thing to note is that the American-Oriental Banking Corporation was originally registered in Connecticut, USA, as a trading company with the same name. When it opened in Shanghai, it operated as a banking business. Mr. He Fu also said that the Pui
