Record of Continuous Muggy Rains, Water Accumulation on Low-Lying Roads Affects Crop Prices 149

The weather in the city has been erratic recently, with frequent sunny and rainy days. The crops, such as rice and cotton, have received enough water. Farmers are eager for sunny weather. However, at 0:30 a.m. yesterday, there was another heavy rain, with raindrops as big as fists, like a downpour. For a time, the roadsides in the Chinese and French Concessions were unable to drain the accumulated water, turning into rivers. Although the rain decreased after 2 a.m., there were still showers until noon, and the rain did not stop until about 1 p.m. The situations in various places are recorded as follows:

Zhabei Area: The roadsides in areas such as Han Bridge, Qujiang Road, Yongxing Road, Yuyingtang Road, and Zhongxing Road were all filled with water in low-lying areas, turning into ditches. The entrances of the shops were all crossed by jumping over boards. The low-lying fields before and after the Xijin Public Office, as well as behind the Quanwan Guild Hall on Gonghe New Road, near the Lu Family Residence on Huta Road, behind the Jiaguo Guild Hall on Taiyang Temple Road, and the open space west of Datong Road south of the Taiyang Temple Railway, were all a vast expanse of water when viewed from a distance due to the lower terrain. The cobblestone roads in various places, such as Zhongxing Road, Gonghe New Road, and Yongxing Road, were all thoroughly cleaned.

A Glimpse of Nanshi

The low-lying areas of Guohuo Road and Difang Ting in Nanshi were all filled with water, several inches deep. By the afternoon, when the rain stopped and the sun came out, the accumulated water in various places gradually receded.

Flight Delay

According to the China National Aviation Corporation, the Shanghai-Hankou West flight was delayed by ten minutes, and the eastbound flight arrived in Shanghai at 2:40 p.m., delayed by forty minutes.

This Year's Rainfall

From January 1 to June 30 this year, the rainfall near the city reached 724 millimeters (28.05 inches), which is 313.2 millimeters more than the 400.8 millimeters (15.78 inches) in the same period last year, reaching nearly two-thirds more. Moreover, from midnight last night to 9 a.m. this morning, another 56.9 millimeters (2.24 inches) of rain was received.

Rice and Wheat Soar

Yesterday, the positions of the upper and lower rice, wheat, and flour Yiyin companies were unimaginable, and it was feared that they would not be able to pay a single cent. As for the American Eastern Banking Company, although a certain amount of money was involved, it is difficult to say whether this amount belongs to it. It is now doing its best to protect the interests of creditors and depositors. Auditor Fulte, under his guidance, is working tirelessly day and night, which is commendable. However, there is still much work to be done. What he has applied to the U.S. Court is to order the defendant to pay the plaintiff the current amount of 188,881.18 yuan, which is equivalent to 135,000 taels in silver, plus the total amount of 6% interest from January 13, 1932 to the date of repayment. The case must eventually be tried, but Chief Judge Helmick, after ordering the defendant to submit a bond on Saturday, went to Beijing on Sunday afternoon to handle the case, and must also go to Tianjin, so it will take about two weeks before he can return to Shanghai to handle this case.

Mr. Raven met with a newspaper reporter at his residence at 555 Hongqiao Road yesterday (Sunday) afternoon and answered questions about the affairs of Pui Yee Bank, American Eastern Banking Company, and American-Oriental Banking Corporation for half an hour. Mr. Raven said that he was surprised that the U.S. Court had issued an order prohibiting him from leaving Shanghai, as he had no intention of leaving Shanghai. The required bond can be prepared today (Monday). However, Raven did not want to reveal the name of the guarantor. When the reporter asked about the 135,000 taels in cash attached to the American-Oriental Banking Corporation in January 1932, Mr. Raven replied that the amount had been properly resolved by the board of directors, and he had consulted with lawyers before accepting it. He firmly believed that the contents of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation at that time and later were substantial. As for the matter of writing off this amount in the books of the American-Oriental Banking Corporation in six years, this was only a matter of bookkeeping, and he felt that there was nothing strange about it. He was not an accountant, and the manager of the bank was a good accountant, and the bank hired a well-known auditor to audit the books. When the American-Oriental Banking Corporation closed its doors, he hoped and believed that the amounts owed to the various accounts could be repaid in full. He still hopes this, but it may take several years. The bank, like many banks in Shanghai, had a large amount of bad debts. However, other banks could transfer funds from their overseas headquarters, while the American-Oriental Banking Corporation's headquarters was located in Shanghai and could not have this convenience. If business improves, the clearing of these bad debts can be accelerated; otherwise, it will take longer. The Pui Yee Bank holds shares in the American Eastern Banking Company, and the American Eastern Banking Company holds shares in the American-Oriental Banking Corporation, so the positions of the first two companies depend on the American-Oriental Banking Corporation. When the reporter asked whether he himself owed money to the Pui Yee Bank, Raven replied that not only did he not owe money, but he also did his best to transfer funds to help it, because the company had more difficulty in turnover than the other two companies, and everything depended on the other two companies.

According to the Shanghai Evening Post, Mr. Raven had not yet found the US$20,000 surety bond or cash required by the U.S. Court by noon today (Monday). This morning, Mr. Raven visited U.S. Court bailiff Fuber to discuss everything. Since Saturday night, Raven's actions have been monitored by representatives of the U.S. Court bailiff. If he still cannot find a guarantor or cash by a certain time this afternoon, he will have to spend the night in the Xiamen Road West Prison.

Transactions were all made on the basis of domestic and foreign floods causing disasters and crop losses, so they rebounded by a dime or so from the previous day. The top grade Tejing (special grade glutinous rice) was 12.8 yuan, the second grade was 12 yuan, and the Tongche (general grade) rebounded by a dime or so. Foreign rice saw a rise of five cents. Wheat opened at 3.54 yuan in the morning, also up a dime. Flour was 2.4 yuan, up more than four cents. Due to the sharp rise in foreign markets, everyone is optimistic. The local gang in this street sees a promising future and is busy with preparations. According to general observations, if the weather continues to be muggy and rainy, then the future market for rice and wheat will have to be looked at higher. As for cotton yarn, yesterday happened to be a holiday, so there was no market. It is expected that the market will also rise when it opens today.

Postponement of Wall Cleaning

In view of the fact that wall advertisements in the city are very messy, the Municipal Health Bureau, in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau, launched a city-wide wall cleaning campaign. All preparations have been completed. It was originally planned to divide the city into seven districts, and the Health Bureau would send personnel to cooperate with the New Life Guidance Team of the Public Security Bureau to start cleaning. According to the Health Bureau, due to the heavy rain yesterday, which was not conducive to work, it was decided to postpone the event. The date will be decided after consultation with the Public Security Bureau.

Second Shanghai North National Products Exhibition Opened Yesterday 150

The Market Will Open Today

The Second Shanghai North National Products Exhibition, organized by the China National Products Manufacturers Association, opened yesterday and the market will open today. The details are recorded separately below.

Organizers of the Conference

The opening ceremony was held at the Zhabei Charitable Organization at 2 p.m. yesterday. More than 70 people attended, including Wang Binyan, Lin Kanghou, Xu Xiaochu, Cai Qiajun, Sun Xinzhu, Liu Zhongying, Ge Futian, and Xu Chengde. Wang Binyan, Lin Kanghou, Cai Qiajun, Sun Xinzhu, and Xu Xiaochu served as the presidium, Liu Zhongying served as the general host, Ge Futian served as the master of ceremonies, and Xu Chengde served as the recorder.

Chairman's Report

After performing the ceremony, Cai Qiajun first reported that this year is the Student National Products Year. The China National Products Manufacturers Association launched the Second National Products Exhibition to implement the purpose of promoting national products so that citizens can have a consistent psychology of loving domestic goods. Nowadays, the way to save our country is to promote domestic goods and resist the dumping of foreign goods. If we only promote domestic goods and do not block the leakage of foreign goods, then its results can be imagined. Since the January 28th Incident, Zhabei's industry and commerce have been declining and have not yet recovered, so we must promote national products to revitalize industry and save the current crisis. I hope that all sectors will assist more to achieve twice the result with half the effort.

Speech and Flag Raising

Then Liu Zhongying gave a speech. It has been three years since our country promoted national products, and its effect is almost zero. The annual leakage is more than hundreds of millions. The reason for this is that the promoters cannot practice what they preach, and can only sing high tunes and shout slogans at the meeting, while the general public in our country mostly respects foreign goods, resulting in this contradictory state. This year is the Student National Products Year. A small number of students have been able to nationalize domestic goods. The Manufacturers Association is afraid that this National Products Year will still become a past phenomenon, so it launched the Second National Products Exhibition. I hope that the people of Shanghai North can understand this purpose. Then Liu Zhongying raised the flag.

Market Open

The temporary market attached to the conference, participated in by domestic product manufacturers, was originally scheduled to open simultaneously yesterday afternoon, but due to continuous muggy rain, construction was not completed, resulting in a postponement to today. The association yesterday issued a notice to the factories, approving opening every day from 9 a.m. to 9 p.m. All participating manufacturers should use the invoices printed by the association, and the staff should wear the association membership card to show uniformity and facilitate identification. The association sells these invoices and badges at face value. The goods sold by each factory are completely based on national products as the standard. If non-national products are found, they will be severely punished according to the regulations.

Dianchun Hall's Opening Postponed

The Municipal Government considers the city's Yimiao (City God Temple) a must-see for Chinese and foreign visitors. However, the Dianchun Hall, Cuixiu Hall, and the inner garden, which embody the spirit of traditional Chinese architecture, have remained closed due to the involvement of various trade associations, which is regrettable. After a meeting convened by the Social Affairs Bureau with representatives from the Public Works, Finance, Public Safety, Land, Education, Public Utilities, and Health Bureaus, as well as the Bean & Rice, Sugar, and Banking Trade Associations, a temporary plan was agreed upon. However, due to the complete use of Dianchun Hall's buildings as the Sugar Industry Elementary School and the small size of the garden, its opening is temporarily postponed. Rubber Industry Petitions Finance Ministry to Limit Factory Output; Drafts Temporary Production Control Plan, Explains Reasons and Requests Announcement for Implementation 153

The Shanghai National Goods Rubber Products Trade Association has petitioned the Ministry of Industry, stating that overproduction within the industry threatens its collapse. They have drafted a temporary plan to regulate supply and demand and request its approval and implementation to provide relief. The rubber products industry is a new one designed to resist foreign imports. Normally, it should be thriving, not facing imminent danger. However, the current reality is that the entire industry is struggling. This is due to the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the depression in the market. The unlimited establishment of factories and unlimited production are fatal flaws. Excessive production impedes economic progress, leading to a myriad of problems: price wars, corner-cutting, and shoddy manufacturing. The impact of this is not only the depletion of capital and the deterioration of goods and credit, but the very foundation of production is being undermined and ultimately destroyed. Therefore, to address the root cause and achieve a quick remedy, production control is necessary to prevent oversupply. This is an immediate, yet essential solution. Furthermore, the Guangzhou Rubber Industry Trade Association has already drafted and implemented a production control method approved by the Guangdong Provincial Government. Article 9 of the association's regulations also contains explicit limitations. Although the specific limitations may differ, the underlying intention is the same. Over the years, overproduction in the industry has unfortunately become a universal problem, requiring an overall rescue plan. Shanghai, with its size and number of businesses, far exceeds Guangzhou. However, there is currently no solution in sight, a situation that is deeply concerning. The association observes that members, scattered like loose sand, are acutely aware of the failures of competition and have seen the positive effects of production limitations in Guangzhou. They have now recognized the need to change course. They have drawn from the Guangzhou Municipal Temporary Measures for Limiting Rubber Shoe Factory Output, as well as Article 9 of the association regulations, and adapted them to Shanghai's circumstances, drafting a plan to control production. This plan has been unanimously approved by the association's representatives at a general meeting. Therefore, they respectfully submit this document to the Ministry, requesting that it be reviewed and approved, and that an official announcement be made and personnel dispatched to oversee its implementation. This will provide relief and the association will be eternally grateful. Submitted to Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, including one copy of the Shanghai National Goods Rubber Products Industry Temporary Production Control Plan and one copy of the Guangzhou Municipal Temporary Measures for Limiting Rubber Shoe Factory Output.

Yongqing Li Disaster Victims' Families Association; Public Burial of Burned Bodies; Election of Officers to Negotiate with Da Zhonghua; City Federation's Four District Branches Discuss Assistance 154

Following the fire at the Da Zhonghua Celluloid Factory, families of the victims of the Yongqing Li disaster held a meeting at 320 Yongqing Li on the afternoon of the previous day at 8:00 PM, attended by over 60 people. Yan Bingzhou presided over the meeting, reporting on the disaster situation. They then discussed and passed the following resolutions: (1) To organize a Da Zhonghua Disaster Victims' Families Support Association, with a registration office at 320 Yongqing Li. (2) To elect Yan Bingzhou as Chairman, Qin Bukun, Liu Jinbiao, and Ni Zirong as Standing Committee Members, Wu Shaowen as Economic Custodian, Yu Tianqu as Accountant, Yan Shaoping as Secretary, and Ying Jiyun, Wu Jin, Yu Shengping, Ying Yuliang, and Ni Yunwu as Supervisors and Negotiating Committee Members. (3) Regarding the public burial of the disaster victims and relief for their families, it was decided that the association would request the Liyi Hall to purchase coffins and clothing for the deceased. The disaster victims' families would be responsible for repaying these costs, except for those in extreme poverty. A fundraising effort of one yuan per household (91 households before the disaster, now 70) would be launched among the non-affected residents of the Li to provide initial relief. (4) To take photographs of the disaster victims' bodies and the tragic situation in the Li. (5) All families of the disaster victims should wait for the coroner's examination of the bodies before hiring vehicles to transport them back to the Li for mourning. (6) Regarding how to address the tragedy, it was decided to hire a lawyer to handle the matter legally. The facts of the incident would be submitted to various organizations and groups to seek justice and request assistance and relief. On the morning of the previous day, over 50 relatives of the deceased hired three trucks to go to the coroner's office on Avenue Petain to collect the bodies in preparation for negotiations with the Da Zhonghua factory. However, the police had received prior notice and, fearing trouble, deployed officers to maintain order. The families insisted on carrying the coffins into the factory, leading to verbal clashes with the police. Eventually, all 16 coffins remained temporarily housed on wasteland next to the Da Zhonghua factory. In the afternoon, the families held an emergency meeting and decided: (1) To send a letter to the Jianghuai Fellow-Villagers Association to convene an emergency meeting to lodge a strong protest and negotiate with the Da Zhonghua Celluloid Factory. (2) Representatives would be dispatched that evening to survey the families, and lawyers would formally file a lawsuit against the Da Zhonghua factory in the First Special Court today, seeking compensation and pensions.

"Please Don't Report to the Police" Robbers Said While Fleeing With Loot; Ningxing Street Tobacco and Paper Store Robbed 155

The Sande Tobacco and Paper Store at No. 66 Ningxing Street (i.e. Caishi Street), east of Zilaihuo Street in the French Concession, is owned by Qian Anren, a Chongming native. Check Bounce Reveals Debt of 15,000 Yuan; Son-in-Law Reluctant to Sue Father-in-Law; Brother Reports to Police 156

Chuan Shaowen, a Ningbo native residing at No. 15, Lane 507, Avenue Mett Herst, is a commission agent for foreign goods and runs Qingfeng Foreign Goods Company. His son-in-law, Li Zhengchu, operates Yuanfengchang Silk and Satin Foreign Cloth Shop at No. 95 McGonigle Road. As both are in the same business and relatives, they frequently interact. Chuan often discounted post-dated checks with his son-in-law Li for cash. Over the months, Chuan's matured checks could not be fully cashed. By April of this year, Chuan owed Li a total of 9,400 yuan in bounced checks. On April 28th, Chuan asked Li to discount three Nanjing Hui checks for 15,000 yuan, 5,000 yuan each, claiming they were not yet due and that he needed the cash for other purposes. He offered three Changfeng Bank checks as collateral. Li, trusting his father-in-law, gave Chuan 5,600 yuan, adding it to the previous debt of 9,400 yuan, totaling 15,000 yuan. Unexpectedly, as the maturity date approached, Li prepared to cash the Changfeng Bank checks, but Chuan, knowing that the three checks for 15,000 yuan were worthless and that there were no funds in the account, asked Li for an extension. However, to this day, nothing has been resolved. Li's brother, Li Yuanchu, reported the matter to the Gordon Road Police Station, requesting the First Special Court to issue an arrest warrant. Yesterday, Chinese Detective Zhu Mengwei and Detective Zhang Liang went and arrested Chuan Shaowen, detaining him at the police station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Goujiu charged him with fraud under Article 339 of the New Criminal Code and issuing bad checks under Article 136 of the Negotiable Instruments Law. He presented the case and the three checks. Li Yuanchu also filed a complaint regarding the previous circumstances. After Judge Liu briefly questioned the defendant, Chuan Shaowen, he ordered him to be detained for further questioning in seven days.

Suspicious Claim of Withdrawal of Attached Shares; Wu's Equity and Payment Date More Than Three Months Apart; Yao Yaoming Sues Wu Jincheng Criminally 157

Yao Yaoming, manager of Chengji Lumber Company at No. 220 Connaught Road, deposited 40,521.48 yuan into the Yikang Fengji Bank on Ningbo Road on January 30th of this year. The bank issued a cashier's check for 36,790.29 yuan. Unexpectedly, on January 31st, the bank suddenly went bankrupt, and the cashier's check could not be cashed. Yao hired lawyer Osen to sue the bank's owner, Wu Jincheng, in the First Special Court for payment. During the lawsuit, Yao discovered that Wu had a large amount of shares in the Rende Bank at No. 3, Lane 138, Tianjin Road. To protect his claim, he requested the court to provisionally attach Wu's shares in Rende. The court approved the provisional attachment. When the ruling was delivered, Rende Bank suddenly claimed that Wu's shares had been withdrawn in February. However, Yao learned that Wu still had significant shares in April. The claim that the shares were withdrawn in February was intended to avoid execution by creditors, which is a violation of Articles 383 and 384 of the Criminal Code. Therefore, Yao hired lawyer Osen to file a criminal lawsuit against Wu. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng of the Fifth Criminal Division of the First Special Court summoned witnesses. The address for Wu Jincheng was listed as No. 377 Jiaozhou Road, but when the bailiff went to serve the summons, that address was the Qingnian Sports Association, and there was no one named Wu Jincheng. Therefore, he could not be summoned. First, Chen Zengrui, manager of Rende Bank, was summoned to testify about whether Wu had shares in Rende Bank. Chen stated that he had 24,000 yuan worth of shares, but that the shares had been withdrawn on February 3rd of this year, and presented the payment book as evidence. Judge Huang examined the book and saw that the date of payment to Wu for 24,000 yuan was May 16th. He asked why the payment date was May 16th if the shares were withdrawn on February 3rd. Chen's answer was vague. Lawyer Osen stated that, according to the plaintiff, Wu's shares were actually worth over 60,000 yuan, but they only claimed 24,000 yuan. The payment date was more than three months after the withdrawal date, and there were several subsequent payments to Wu in the book after May 16th. The book was full of irregularities and should be temporarily held for examination. Chen Guoliang was the lawyer receiving summonses for Wu Jincheng's civil case, so summonses for this case should be sent to Chen for forwarding. Judge Huang approved this and stated that further investigation was needed, so the case would be adjourned for further hearing.

Double Suicide at Far East Hotel; Suicide Note Cites Lack of Marital Freedom; Overdose Threatens Lives 161

A young couple arrived at the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road on the day before yesterday (29th). Arm in arm, they booked room 404 on the fourth floor. The register listed the man as Shen Zhongkang from Ningbo, age 30. The woman was simply listed as Ms. Shen, age 20, wearing a purplish-brown cheongsam. They stayed for two days without going out. On the previous night, they went out together briefly, returning around 11:00 PM. Before going to bed, they told the room service attendant that they needed to get up early at 10:00 AM the next morning and asked him to knock on the door to wake them up. The attendant agreed and left, closing the door tightly. The next morning, at 10:00 AM, the attendant knocked on the door, but there was no response. Becoming suspicious, he forced the door open and saw the couple lying in bed, staring blankly, barely breathing. Several empty bottles of tranquilizer pills were on the table, along with four suicide notes. The notes stated that they were not free to marry and would rather die. Realizing that they had likely taken poison, he rushed to tell the front desk, which then reported it to the Laoza Police Station. They were rushed to Renji Hospital by ambulance. Due to the large overdose, their lives were in danger.

Tobacco Dealers Association Notifies Members to Prevent Selling of Counterfeit Cigarettes; Autumn Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Opens - Apply for Renewal Immediately 163

The Shanghai Tobacco Dealers Association's South Shanghai Office issued three notices yesterday: (1) Regarding the matter of notification, according to regulations, the collection period for the autumn tobacco and alcohol license tax is from July 1st to 10th. All members should promptly send employees to the office with their old licenses and tax payment to renew them. If a store has no employees to send, they should submit their old licenses and tax payment to the office's collector for renewal. Failure to do so may result in penalties, so please do not ignore this matter. This notice. (2) Regarding the matter of notification, according to recent investigations, some people in this district are selling counterfeit Fairy Brand and various other counterfeit cigarettes to various stores. Members, lured by cheap prices, mistakenly accepted them, and were discovered by the tax office and heavily fined. Given the current difficult living conditions, it is unbearable to suffer further losses. Therefore, this notice is to urge all members to be vigilant. If anyone comes to your store to sell the aforementioned counterfeit cigarettes, refuse to buy them and immediately report them to the office so that they can be sent to the authorities for strict punishment according to the law. When purchasing goods, please only purchase from wholesale merchants and do not be fooled by others, or you will suffer unexpected losses. Be careful. This notice. (3) Regarding the matter of notification, the gifts for Red Sister Brand cigarettes produced by He Xing Tobacco Company are Invincible Brand soap in Shanghai and their own brand of cigarettes in other cities. According to a request from members, Invincible Brand soap is not selling well, so they requested the same treatment as other cities, switching to their own brand of cigarettes to promote sales. The office sent representatives to negotiate with the company, and they agreed to accommodate this request, allowing members to choose whether to exchange for soap or cigarettes at their discretion. This notice is to inform all members. In the future, when you have accumulated gifts from the company, you can specify which type of gift you want to receive when you claim them from the company. This notice.

Yangshupu Robbery Case: Fierce Robbers Detained Awaiting Further Investigation 168

Previously, Detective Chief Sun and Detective Su, who were handling the case at the Yangshupu police station, went to the Second Special Court and brought the four robbers, Liu, Tang, Chen, and Lin, back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Attorney Wang Yaotang of the Public Works Department recounted the previous events, stating that the defendant Liu Yulong had admitted at the police station to having conspired with Li Si, Wu Zhongxing, Xu Guangrong, and others, who are still at large, in the robbery case at Chen Buzhao's home in Fulu Lane, Yangshupu Road, and admitted to shooting and wounding Chen, Zhang, and Shi. Tang Bingguang was identified at the police station by the victims, Zhang Jin Yang and Shi Jinshi, as being present at the scene. The handgun Liu Yulong carried in the French Concession robbery had the number 15084, Huang's brand, and its bullets were the same as those that wounded Chen Buzhao. However, the gun was not brought and requested the court to send a letter to the Second Special Court, the police station would send detectives to collect it. As for the two defendants, Chen and Lin, they should be detained and investigated regarding the Chen Buzhao case and requested an extension. The police station's statement from Liu was presented for review. Judge Jiang Shuzi questioned the defendants and ordered them to be returned to detention for further investigation at a later date.

Sawmill Workers Violate Regulations: A Brawl Ensues 169

The Shanghai White and Red Wood Industry Workers' Union recently resolved that all stores purchasing wood must have it delivered to the store by traders and then notify the sawmill workers to come and saw it. The union also restricted workers from transporting wood themselves from the traders' carts. There was a worker named Ji Zihai from Jiangbei, 43 years old, residing at No. 24, Lane 57, Sangyuan Street outside Xiaonanmen, who worked as a sawmill worker. Yesterday, Ji was hired by Wang Renji's Wood Shop and went to the Taijiang Wood Firm, transported a section of redwood home in a cart, and began to saw it. Unexpectedly, he was spotted by his fellow worker Yu Changcheng (40 years old, from Wenzhou) from No. 15 in the same lane, who believed Ji was deliberately violating the union's regulations. So, yesterday morning around 8 a.m., Yu gathered over forty fellow workers from the Wenzhou gang and rushed to Ji's home to prevent him from sawing the wood. Ji refused and also gathered over twenty fellow workers from the Jiangbei gang, and they argued with each other. When the two sides disagreed, they each grabbed wooden sticks and started a brawl. The Patrol Street Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau was informed and immediately dispatched a large number of patrol officers who rushed to the scene and arrested the ringleaders, Ji and Yu, along with over twenty workers from both gangs. However, several people were injured, and the rest fled. The officers then brought the arrested individuals back to the station, where Director Jin interrogated them separately. Considering the case involved a large-scale brawl, he ordered a written report to be prepared and sent to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Chen Yishun, a native of Chuansha, operated a milk shed at No. 7, Guojiawan, south of Caohejing Town in the West Shanghai. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Zhang Zi of the court arrived at the scene with the coroner for examination. The coroner found that the deceased was wearing a blue linen short shirt and trousers with a straw raincoat, and a copper basin hat. The examination confirmed that he died from internal injuries caused by being kicked by a cow. He filled out the death certificate and ordered the family to prepare a coffin for burial pending further investigation.

Public Concession Bureau of Health Report

Sports News

The Organizing Committee of the Current National Games Announces: Summary of New Rules for the Track and Field All-Around Competition; Also Announces Rules for Women's Javelin Throw Demonstration 183

The Organizing Committee of the Sixth National Games issued its second announcement yesterday, which included a summary of the new rules for track and field all-around competitions, race walking, and women's softball throw, as well as points to note when registering with various units. The details are as follows:

Summary of New Rules for the Track and Field All-Around Competition

The international sports associations have made slight modifications to the rules for track and field events and all-around sports. In addition, the rules for women's softball throwing were previously lacking in our track and field competition rules. They are now included together with the new rules and explained as follows:

(A) Modification of Timing Methods: For timing in track races, any fraction of a second less than one second was previously calculated as one-tenth of a second for distances of 250 meters or less, and as one-fifth of a second for distances greater than 250 meters. The International Sports Association has now decided that for track distances of 1,000 meters or less, the fraction of a second will be calculated as one-tenth of a second, and for distances greater than 1,000 meters, it will be calculated as one-fifth of a second.

(B) Modification of Hurdling Rules: A new note has been added to Article 6 of Chapter 38, 110-meter hurdles, with the full text as follows:

(Note) If new hurdles are used, the following provisions shall apply:

An athlete who knocks down one or more hurdles will not be disqualified, and the resulting score may be recognized as an official record. According to the resolution of the International Sports Association conference held in Stockholm, the capital of Sweden, in 1934, new and old hurdles of all types can be used until the end of 1936. The World Games to be held in Berlin, Germany, in 1936 will use the new hurdles. (The same applies to 400-meter hurdles)

In addition, a new section on the construction of new hurdles has been added to Chapter 53, with the full text as follows:

The hurdle is made of wood or metal, with two bases and two posts, supported by a rectangular frame. The frame can use one or several horizontal bars for strength. The posts are each installed at one end of the base, and the height of the hurdle can be raised or lowered arbitrarily, but there must be a way to stop it at various heights. The structure of the hurdle is legally overturned when a force of 3.6 kilograms (8 pounds) or more is applied to the center of the hurdle. The top is painted with alternating black and white diagonal stripes.

Height: The height of the hurdle is detailed in the rules. Hurdle dimensions: 1.20 meters (3 feet 11 inches) high, base length 70 cm (27.5 inches), each hurdle weighs at least 10 kilograms (22.22 pounds).

Placement: The hurdle should be placed with the end of the base with the post at the front, i.e., the side closer to the finish line, and the empty end of the base facing the starting line.

(C) Softball Throwing Rules: Chapter 60, "Softball Throwing," has been added to the track and field rules, with the full text as follows:

Article 1: The softball should be thrown from behind the throwing line. The construction of the throwing line is the same as for the javelin throw.

Article 2: The diameter of the softball is 30 cm (12 inches). When throwing the softball, it should be thrown with one hand over the shoulder. Throwing from the side or diagonally is invalid.

Article 3: When throwing the softball, the feet must not touch the throwing line.

Article 4: The athlete must not cross the throwing line before the ball lands.

Article 5: The distance is measured at a right angle from the closest point where the ball lands to the inner edge of the throwing line or its extension. (Note) The referee may instruct the athlete to lightly coat the ball with lime before throwing to easily identify the landing point.

Article 6: All articles of Chapter 32 that are relevant to this chapter shall apply.

(D) Modification of Scoring Tables for the Decathlon and Pentathlon

The old scoring tables for the decathlon and pentathlon had the problem of addition and subtraction calculations during inspection. The Finnish Sports Association has now drafted new ones, which were adopted at the International Sports Association conference held in Stockholm, the capital of Sweden, in 1934. This table has a wider range of applications. The score that should be given for any result can be found with a quick check, without the need for addition and subtraction calculations, saving time and effort, and avoiding the drawbacks of scoring errors. In addition, this scoring table has another advantage, namely that the level of scoring is lower than the old one, so items with poorer results will not be without points, which will prevent athletes from feeling disappointed. This new scoring table has been printed into the track and field competition rules of the conference and will be distributed to various units for use in mid-July.

Race Walking Demonstration Distance and Rules

(A) Distance

The distances for the race walking demonstration competition at this conference are temporarily set at 50,000 meters and 30,000 meters, to be held on two days. Both will be held on the road, but the starting and ending points will be within the track and field stadium. The route will be measured and announced later with a map.

(B) Rules

(Definition) When an athlete is moving, the feet move forward and backward, alternately touching the ground, without both feet leaving the ground at the same time. This is called race walking and is the main difference from running. Therefore, the rules for race walking are only two very simple ones: (1) When one foot moves forward, the knee joint must be straight when the heel touches the ground and not bent. (2) The foot behind must only be lifted to move forward after the foot in front has touched the ground. (For example, when the left foot moves forward, the knee joint must be straight when it touches the ground. This is the inevitable result of a legal walking step. Only after the left foot has touched the ground can the right foot be lifted and moved forward. If the right foot is lifted before the left foot has touched the ground, the whole body will naturally be in the air, which is running, which is not consistent with the definition of race walking and constitutes a foul.)

Article 1: During a race walking competition, if a referee believes that an athlete's walking method is about to be a foul but has not yet constituted a foul, he may first give a warning.

Article 2: During a race walking competition, if two referees both believe that an athlete's walking method does not conform to the definition of race walking, he should be immediately disqualified, and any one of the two referees should give a formal notification to the athlete who committed the foul. If it is not possible to notify the athlete who was disqualified for a foul in a timely manner, it may be carried out immediately after the competition is over, and its effect is the same as notifying it when the foul occurred.

Article 3: If the competition is held on the track, the athlete must leave the track immediately when he is notified of the disqualification. If the competition is held on the road, the athlete must automatically remove the number cloth prepared when he is notified of the disqualification.

(Note) During a race walking competition, it is best to use various signals for notification, such as raising a white flag to indicate a warning and raising a red flag to indicate disqualification, so that all staff, athletes, and spectators can easily understand. However, this signal is not required in the competition.

Key Points of Women's Softball Rules

(1) Each unit must fill out the type of event to be participated in on the form and send it to the meeting before September 10. This procedure is necessary to estimate the number of participants from each unit and to arrange the order of the ball games. Only after receiving this registration form can the association estimate the number of participants from each unit and calculate the dormitory location in advance, so that it can cope with it comfortably and avoid the disadvantages of cramped and unsuitable accommodation. The order of the ball games can also be arranged in advance, so as to avoid the rush in printing the order and the occurrence of inconsistencies. Therefore, it is hoped that each unit will not regard this registration procedure as unimportant and ignore it. Overseas or remote units may use telegraph registration if time is limited, but it should be described clearly so that no errors occur. In addition, each unit should pay close attention to the provisions of Article 33 of Chapter 19 of the competition rules and consider it carefully in advance.

(2) Each unit must send the complete registration form for all athletes to the association before September 20, so that the preliminary classification can be arranged and everything related to the competition can be published in detail in the order book. This form is printed into a book, and each page can be written in triplicate at the same time with carbon paper. Each unit should tear off the first two sheets of each page, divide them into two copies and send them to the association, and keep the remaining one copy for reference. In the previous National Games, the registration of athletes from each unit was heard to be done by telegraph, and the descriptions were not clear enough, and there were many errors in the text. Not only was it difficult for the office to handle the matter, but each unit also felt inconvenient after the errors occurred. Therefore, when registering this year, each unit hopes to fill out and send the official forms issued by the association in accordance with the provisions of Article 34 of Chapter 19 of the competition rules. When sending the forms, each unit also hopes to consider the time required for mailing and send them out with sufficient time before the deadline, so that the association can receive them in a timely manner and avoid delaying the allocation work and the compilation and printing of the order book. To achieve this, all remote units and overseas Chinese groups should hold preliminary elections before the end of August, and immediately select representatives, fill out the forms and send them.

(3) The athlete number cloths for the track and field competitions, all-around sports, swimming, martial arts, and various demonstration competitions of each unit will be prepared by the association and issued according to the number of people on the registration form when each unit reports. Therefore, please do not fill in the athlete number grids for the above competitions in the registration form yourself.

(4) Number cloths for ball game athletes will not be issued separately. Therefore, when making uniforms, each unit must make the number and unit name at the same time, and the number of ball game athletes should be filled in by each unit on the registration form. Each unit should pay special attention to this, and when ordering the uniforms of each athlete, the number should be consistent with the one filled in on the registration form. This matter is extremely necessary for the competition and for the audience, and it is hoped that each unit will implement it in accordance with the law.

(5) Conflicts in the timing of various competitions are virtually unavoidable. Therefore, each unit should select athletes carefully.

(6) The association plans to divide the track and field competition schedule into six days this time, in order to reduce the difficulty of athletes participating in several events at the same time and to achieve better results. Therefore, if athletes participate in events that are reasonable, there should be no conflicts or excessive fatigue. The all-around sports are planned to be held for two days, following the track and field competition. Swimming is planned to be held for five days, starting at the same time as the all-around sports. Units with athletes who participate in both all-around and swimming should pay attention to this.

(7) Ball games will be very crowded in the first few days, but the association is determined to try its best to ensure that no two competitions are held at the same time for each unit in the preliminary rounds. However, after the preliminary rounds, the outcome of each week is difficult to predict, and it is inevitable that they will be held at the same time. Each unit should carefully consider the players who have two or more types of games.

(8) According to the provisions of Article 16 (a) of Chapter 9 of the tennis competition rules, the tennis players should be filled in according to the level of each player's skills in the order of first singles, second singles, etc. In the future, when attending the competition, if the first singles cannot play, the second singles should be promoted to fill in, and any one of the remaining four people should be supplemented as the second singles. If both the first and second singles do not attend, then they should still be supplemented in order, and no reversal is allowed. Therefore, each unit should pay attention to this when filling out the form, and it is hoped that each will arrange it sincerely. As for doubles, it can be composed of any two people. Regardless of singles or doubles, once the first competition is over, the players who attend can no longer be replaced.

(9) There is a athlete event comparison table for track and field competitions, all-around sports, and martial arts. Each unit must fill it out according to the format and send it together with other registration forms. Because there is a fixed quota for the number of items that each athlete joins and the number of athletes who join each item for the above competitions, this comparison table can avoid errors in the number. Therefore, you should not be afraid of being bothered and fill out the form according to the table for easy reference. If the comparison table filled out by each unit does not match the registration form, the association will base it on the registration form. If an athlete participates in more items than the quota, or if more athletes participate in an item than the quota, the association may arbitrarily cancel any item or any person, and each unit shall not object.

(10) Relay races in women's track and field competitions and men's and women's swimming are not within the fixed quota of participating items. In other words, those who participate in relay races can have a maximum of five items. In addition, six people can be filled in when registering for relays, and any four of them can attend during the competition, but after preparation, the semi-finals and finals must still be attended by these four people, and no changes are allowed.

(11) There is a fixed quota for various ball game players, and no more can be filled in. Otherwise, the association may arbitrarily remove any one or several people, and those who are under quota will listen. However, after registration, no request can be made to add up to the fixed number.

(12) If there are any deletions or changes on various registration forms, the person in charge should add a seal on the bottom page (that is, the originally written page) to show solemnity.

(13) The number of staff and athletes in each unit shall be limited to what is filled in on the registration form. The association's reception and issuance of badges will be based on this.

(14) If an athlete who has been registered in each unit cannot attend due to some reason, the competent authority may prepare an official letter and apply to the association for replacement before September 30. It will be invalid after the deadline (the date of the Shanghai Post Office stamp shall prevail), and this replacement is only limited to athletes, not the items to be participated in. Therefore, the replaced athlete should still participate in the items that the original registered athlete intended to participate in, and no other items can be changed or new items added.

(15) In addition to the above registration forms, the association also prepares a personal registration certificate for athletes. Each unit should instruct the athletes to fill it out according to the style, striving for details, and attach a 2.5-inch half-length photo for reference. This athlete registration certificate can be brought to the association when each unit reports and does not need to be sent.

Conference Accommodation Arrangements: Meals are Arranged by Each Unit; Accommodation is Provided by the Conference 184

The number of participants in this conference is expected to be very enthusiastic, and it is not possible to eat together at the same time. Therefore, each meal is divided into two openings (the type, price, and time are indicated on the meal ticket). The types and prices of the three meals are listed below:

(A) Breakfast: Congee and pickled vegetables, 8 people per table, price 1 yuan. If you add 20 steamed buns, add another 4 jiao.

(B) Lunch and Dinner: Dishes are divided into 5 types: Ordinary, Jiangsu, Sichuan, Cantonese, and Halal, with 8 people per table. The prices are divided into 2.4 yuan, 3 yuan, 4 yuan, and 5.4 yuan.

The meals for the athletes and staff of each unit shall be arranged by the respective units. However, the above-mentioned dishes must be decided in advance and contracted to reliable restaurants. Each unit is requested to inform the association in writing of the number of people and the type and price of dishes required two weeks before the opening of the conference, so that the overall plan can be made. After the delegation reports, the fee must be paid to the catering department of the general affairs section of the association before 5 pm every day to receive the meal tickets for the next day (divided into table tickets and individual tickets), so that the contractor can be notified to prepare in advance, so as to avoid being caught short in an emergency and the drawbacks of surplus or insufficient food. If each unit is dissatisfied with the meals provided, it can report to the staff of the catering department, and it is hoped that it will not be handled directly.

Regarding the meals of the referees of the conference, lunch will be provided by the association on the spot. Each person will be issued a meal ticket for lunch, and they can sit and eat with the ticket. They can eat individually or with several people. The cafeteria is separated from the athletes. Breakfast and dinner for out-of-town referees will be provided by the association at the accommodation. Breakfast and dinner for local referees will not be provided.

The meals for the audience will be arranged by the conference in designated locations and rented to various restaurants and vendors. The audience can buy food freely, but the restaurants that contract to provide meals for the conference are restricted from soliciting these yellow customers.

The accommodation for the athletes and staff of each unit will be planned by the conference as a whole, and the dormitory of the venue will be allocated for residence. All related personnel of each unit who are not within the scope of the association's reception shall not be allowed to stay. The daily necessities of each athlete and staff member shall be prepared by themselves.

Chronicle

Tidbits 203

— (Lan Shan)

In the courtroom, the plaintiff and defendant eloquently stated their cases, recounting the details of the matter. Then, lawyers from both sides presented various pieces of evidence, refuting each other's claims. It was truly a case of "the public has its reasons, and the wife has her reasons." At that time, onlookers could only listen and observe, finding it difficult to know which side was right or wrong. Only after several trials did the truth come to light. The winning party breathed a sigh of relief and beamed with joy, while the losing party hung their head in dejection. This moment reveals the existence of "right" and "wrong" in the world, and it is the most precious instant.

Kidnappers, robbers, and others who have committed serious crimes deserving of death have not completely extinguished their "conscience." On the day of execution, after eating a few farewell steamed buns and drinking a cup of parting wine, they feel the terror of impending death. Thinking about their past mistakes and the inevitable punishment of the law, their hearts awaken at this moment, followed by remorse and tears. They yearn for this colorful and strange life. Who can comprehend even a fraction of the sorrow of their state of mind at this time? Their repentance is necessary, but it is too late. (Why not carefully consider the consequences before committing the crime?)

Superstitions About Smoking 204

— Zhou Xian

Foreigners often say that Chinese people are superstitious, but in fact, there are countless superstitious beliefs among foreigners as well. Taking the act of smoking cigarettes as an example, foreigners have ten times more superstitions than Chinese people.

In the rural areas of northern Scotland, there is a popular and unbelievable belief that if a cigarette that is being smoked suddenly goes out on its own, the smoker will encounter great misfortune in the near future. If the cigarette comes unglued and bursts open while being smoked, it is a sign that the smoker will commit a crime and be imprisoned. In western Spain, along the Atlantic coast, residents absolutely refuse to share a cigarette. Their superstition is that if two people share a cigarette, the first smoker's wife will commit adultery. Before the revolution in Russia, people also had a widespread superstition that if a cigarette butt thrown on the ground burned completely, good luck would come, but if it did not burn completely, it did not signify bad luck, but only that unexpected good fortune would not be obtained. In Hungary in the late nineteenth century, it was popular to tell fortunes about future husbands or wives by smoking cigarettes. Generally, a cigarette that could be smoked smoothly and effortlessly would lead to a satisfactory partner in the near future. If a cigarette had to be relit, came unglued, burst open, or burned in a distorted way, it was a sign of an unsuccessful marriage.

In China, the fire on a cigarette cannot be given to someone else to light another cigarette, especially among gamblers, who consider it a great taboo, saying that if someone else takes your fire, you will definitely lose money gambling.

God of Wealth, A Wu 205

— Rong Yu

"God of Wealth, A Wu" was not a wealthy millionaire, but a beggar who went door to door. He was able to have this name only after undergoing three transformations. First: everyone called him "Young Master Wu." Needless to say, at this time, he was a playboy enjoying the blessings of his parents. Second: everyone called him "Wu Xiang," because at this time, his fields had been sold off, and his house had been sold. He lived by borrowing money. Third: only then did he have the name "A Wu." At this time, his wife had also run away with someone else. He relied on a bamboo pole and a broken basket, begging from door to door. However, I was somewhat puzzled by the addition of "God of Wealth" to "A Wu." If it was to commemorate his past wealth, then there were many royal descendants in the humble fields. If it was to mock him, he may have been extravagant in his youth, but he may not have done evil. Why be so harsh on him? Later, I asked the elderly and learned the origin of the name "God of Wealth."

It turned out that his father was a great wealthy man in his lifetime. However, he was stingy by nature and would not help anyone, and he might have been very harsh to people. After the age of fifty, he only had four daughters and no sons. In the past, daughters had no right to inherit property, and he was afraid that no one would offer sacrifices after his death, so he always wanted to have a son. He was a person who did somersaults in the eyes of money, so he worshiped the God of Wealth at home, and he also burned incense to the God of Wealth at temples. He prayed to the God of Wealth day and night. In his dream, he saw the God of Wealth rewarding him with a silver ingot, laughing heartily, but waking up, it was just a dream, and Young Master Wu was born at this time.

He thought that the God of Wealth had bestowed the gift, and he would definitely become the second "Shen Wansan" in the future, so he did not teach him to study, nor did he teach him a trade, letting him roam and waste his time. Later, when he closed his eyes, "Young Master Wu" gradually turned into "God of Wealth, A Wu"!

"Leaving wealth to descendants is not as good as leaving education to descendants." After learning about the life of God of Wealth, A Wu, I believe even more that this saying is true.

Sharp Answers 206

— (Master of Qifeng Building)

Lawyer and Accountant: The current market is truly terrible! We hear news of shops, companies, and other businesses declaring liquidation every day. All industries are so depressed. What are we going to do?

Merchant: You can't generalize like that. The business of you two has increased a lot.

Patriot: Today's China faces internal troubles and external threats, with frequent disasters. Last year there was a drought, and recently there have been floods in several places. The nation is burdened with calamity upon calamity. When will we ever have peaceful days again?

Humorist: I think that China will definitely become peaceful and prosperous in the near future! Because the ancients said, "A nation is strengthened by adversity."

Little Western Paradise 207

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Fifteen: Kind Words Do Not Calm the Empty Table; Money and Lights Piteously Sell People

Bei Hai lowered his head and wiped up the spilled tea on the tea table. He didn't look up until the waiter had left. Zhi Qian smiled: Miss Yang said that nothing moves people more than sincere words. We managed to pull Miss Zhu out of a difficult situation, so your enthusiasm wasn't for nothing. Bei Hai looked pleased. Zhi Qian continued: I have more good news. Magistrate Zhou is very enthusiastic. He said that if you marry her, he's willing to help you financially. Bei Hai found a piece of paper under the tea table and wiped his hands. Zhi Qian poured a cup of tea and asked, "If you're really determined, you should talk to your parents and then come talk to me." Bei Hai paused for a moment, then stood up and said, "There's nothing to talk about." After saying only five words, he fell silent. They sat in silence for a while. Bei Hai felt bored, so he asked: Did you want to see me today to discuss something, Mr. Cheng? Zhi Qian replied: What I wanted to say, I just said. First, I want to make it clear that I have no intentions. Second, I advise you to consider it. Bei Hai said: I don't have anything... He didn't finish what he wanted to say, his voice was very soft, and he stopped. Zhi Qian smiled: If there's something you don't want to discuss in front of people today, we can talk about it another day. Bei Hai said it was getting late and bid farewell to return to school. Zhi Qian sat in the room, feeling a great deal of emotion. He propped up his head, sat at the table, and just thought aimlessly. He didn't know how much time had passed, but he heard the sound of silver dollars falling to the ground. (254)

The Misty Records of Imperial Incense 208

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Finally, the four imperial physicians completed their pulse-taking work. At almost the same time, they suddenly got up, kowtowed to the Empress Dowager as usual, and tiptoed out of the inner palace. The Empress Dowager did not speak directly to them but said to me:

"Der Ling, you go out with them and keep an eye on them!"

Her tone was still very sharp, obviously because she had not completely suppressed her anger! But her intention in telling me to go out was not because of this. Judging from her daily actions, I suspected that she did not fully trust the four imperial physicians. So, I quickly obeyed and followed the four imperial physicians into a side hall adjacent to the Empress Dowager's bedroom. There, four small, low tables and chairs had been set up in advance, with pens, inkstones, paper, and ink placed on the tables. The four imperial physicians each occupied a seat and sat down respectfully. First, each of them silently wrote a set of pulse records. After finishing the set of pulse records, they began to discuss them, each expressing their own opinions. As a result, the four people had four different opinions, none of which were the same. This was certainly not acceptable! The four people then tried their best to compromise, agreed on a consensus, and destroyed the first set of pulse records, replacing them with a set of largely identical phrases. The Empress Dowager's condition was determined by such speculation and discussion! Next, the four physicians had to come up with their own prescriptions. When writing the prescriptions, they seemed to be even more solemn than when writing the pulse records. Each of them pondered and murmured, working as diligently as students facing a major exam. It took them a long time to complete the task. However, they no longer discussed the use of medication but came up with their own ideas. As a result, four different prescriptions were produced. (354)

Local Customs and Anecdotes

Sketches of Japanese Customs 209

— Yan

Men and Women Living Together in the Natsudomari Tribe

In the Natsudomari tribe of Ketaka County, Tottori Prefecture, Japan, there are a total of 70 households with 450 people. Because it is close to the Sea of Japan, everyone relies on fishing for a living. Every year from June 1st to September 15th is the fishing season. Women aged 15 to 30 are very busy during that season, competing to catch fish. The men stay at home to sort the fish and shellfish and sell them to various villages and towns. In the autumn, gathering aromatic herbs is also the only side business for the women of the Natsudomari tribe, and the income is not small.

In the Natsudomari tribe, there are three customs that are different from other places: the nationally famous men and women living together, praying for the birth of girls, and collective pilgrimages.

Men and women living together is called "Wakashu Yado" or [blank space] [blank space] in Japanese, which means young men and women living together. In a large room, a folding screen divides the space into two rooms, with a large stove placed in the gap of the screen. After dinner, the young men and women each bring two or three bundles of firewood or four or five pieces of charcoal and come to the large stove in the room. The men and women sit together, chat and laugh, shake hands and nudge shoulders, without any restrictions. The men either knit fishing nets or repair furniture, while the women either make shoes and hats or sew clothes. When the night is late, the men go to one room on the left, and the women go to the room on the right, each going to sleep.

Because of this custom, the sexuality of young men and women is liberated before marriage, and the harm of early maturity is inevitable. Early marriage has become the norm in the entire village. Almost no girls over the age of fourteen and no boys over the age of sixteen are virgins. After a physical relationship has occurred and they get along well, they get permission from their parents and then hold a formal wedding ceremony. Therefore, there are many illegitimate children in this village, but once they get married, there are never any divorce tragedies.

The custom of praying for the birth of girls is considered extremely strange in Japan. Because almost all parts of Japan are biased in favor of boys over girls, women are generally respected in this village. Therefore, every woman, after being three months pregnant, goes to the local shrine to worship, either with the village leader or with her husband, to pray for a safe birth and a strong and beautiful girl.

If they know it's a girl at the time of delivery, not only is the whole family happy, but the people of the entire village are very happy. When the girl turns four, she must be thrown into the sea during the summer festival. So, before the summer festival, the parents must teach the girl to swim every day so that she is not harmed.

Collective pilgrimages are also called [blank space] [blank space] by the Japanese. The residents of this village often gather ten or twenty people each year, and sometimes even forty or fifty people as a group, to take a long trip together. Although the destination of the trip is not fixed, it is always mainly temples and shrines, mostly in the Shikoku area and the Shodo Island area. As for the metropolises such as Tokyo, Kyoto, and Osaka, they have probably never been to one, so they simply do not know the most developed state of Japanese culture. However, after traveling once, they can add a lot of new material when men and women sit around the stove talking and laughing on long winter nights. Everyone often tells each other about the beautiful women they encountered in the various hotels. I don't know if the women in that village feel any jealousy after hearing this?

Foodstuffs: Excessive Rainfall Causes Flour and Wheat to Rise Together 211

The flour market has seen universal and rapid increases. The price of imported wheat rose by one dollar yesterday, but today it only increased by around forty-eight to twenty cents. The Yangtze River and Jiangsu-Zhejiang areas are experiencing excessive mold-inducing rains, leading to concerns about potential flooding. People cannot help but worry deeply about the future of food supplies. On Sunday, Tianjin also managed to trade 60,000 to 70,000 bags of Fufeng spot goods, with prices already reaching 2.435 dollars per bag (more than seven and a half cents higher than the July closing price). Due to these various reasons, everyone expects prices to be high. Both domestic and out-of-town merchants are buying in large quantities, leading to an average market increase of four to five cents. However, factories have been selling off some stock, and the quantity is considerable. By the afternoon opening, the weather seemed to be clearing up, so out-of-town merchants' buying interest decreased relatively. Factories continued to sell, and speculators also resold. Therefore, near and far-term prices fell by about one cent. Observing the future trend, if the weather does not clear up, people will still have positive expectations, and the market will likely remain stable. As a result, this month's price rose by three and a half cents, next month's by four cents, September's by three cents and seven mills, October's by two cents and seven mills. December has already been sold, initially opening at four dollars and eight cents, and closing down by seven mills.

Considering the environment, people are greatly shaken. Therefore, opening prices immediately rose by six, seven, or eight cents. Later, the price fluctuated less. Trading remained brisk in the afternoon because the flour market slightly declined, and people's enthusiasm also seemed weaker. The current wheat market prices, due to the rain and the increase in standards, are also rising by five or six cents.
