Free Talk

Articles Without an Attitude 225

— Ling Jing

"Without an attitude" means that the author, whether describing a story or narrating a theory, does not express his own opinions about the story or theory at all. In other words, the author stands completely in a "purely objective" position, without any subjective opinions being mixed in. Is such an article possible?

This question has already been answered by someone, but despite the answer, practitioners are still using it. Advertisements stating that "the author stands in an objective position, narrates the course of events, and does not include any subjective opinions, truly a rare work" can still be seen everywhere. Even critics use such words to tout the value of the original work. I think this kind of specious concept is like opium, poisoning the brains and blood of young people.

I don't want to use any laws or theories to answer this question. Let's look at a few simple examples. For example, we write in an arithmetic textbook, "Two plus two equals four." This seems to be very objective and does not contain any subjective opinions, but it is not. It is true that "two plus two equals four" is an objective truth, but when we write it in a book, we are not just blindly copying it. First, it must be approved by our subjective judgment before we write it. If we subjectively believe that two plus two equals five, would we still be willing to write it as two plus two equals four? Another example is that most of the young women appearing in novels are described as beautiful and charming, but in reality, are there so many beautiful women? The reason is that humans have a subjective aesthetic sense of loving beauty and hating ugliness, so even if the woman the author wants to portray (naturally still a woman in the author's imagination) originally only has three parts beauty, it turns out to be ten parts beauty when written on paper.

In short, whether it is science or literature, as long as it is a text written on paper, it must contain the author's subjective opinions (there is only a difference in the amount of subjective components). There is no purely objective text in the world, but there are purely subjective works. Such purely subjective things are naturally worthless, just like the ravings of a madman. A valuable work—whether it is science or literature—must have the author's subjective opinions precisely matching the objective truth. In other words, it must be completed in the unified category of subject and object.

The Moon-Worshipping Pavilion and the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool 226

— Wo Pu

The Moon-Worshipping Pavilion was involved in a public case during the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty. Shen Defu's Guqu Zayan's comments on the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion say:

"In the past, in the year Gui Si, the young masters of Wu practiced martial arts, and were accused by the Jiangnan Pacification Commissioner Zhu Jiantang, saying that the young masters were about to rebel, and the poem they gave to their guests, 'You really have the heart to chase Ji Bu, but the humble home has no way to entrust Zhu Jia' was used as definite proof of rebellion. Censor Zhao Wanbi reported it to the emperor accordingly. At that time, the three ministers were all from Wu and Yue, fearing that the emperor would believe it to be true, they urgently requested to send Pacification Commissioners to investigate the truth. Zhu had already left office, and someone interceded for him, saying: This is from the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion opera, Tuo Man Xingfu gave it to Jiang Shilong, and Jiang gave this sentence in reply, not the creator. So they took the carved version from the market to prove it, and it was indeed so. The young masters' prison gradually dissolved, and Wang Fangzhong was also one of the young masters. Now, reading the new and old carved versions carefully, there is no such couplet. Could it be that when the great prison arose, they hated its implication and removed these two sentences? Or it is said: The Moon-Worshipping Pavilion originally had no such poem, but the resolver pretended to say this as a 'liaocheng arrow,' is that so?"

In Tan Qian's Zaolin Miscellaneous Congzheng's "Zhu Zhongcheng Mistakenly Reported Anti-Poetry" entry, there is also a similar record:

"Zhu Hongmo opened the mansion in Wuzhong. At that time, Guanbai was very alert. Wang Shi County of Taicang and others practiced archery in groups, or someone accused them of rebellion, and the manuscript 'You really have the heart to chase Ji Bu, but the humble home has no way to entrust Zhu Jia' was taken as evidence. Hongmo reported it to the emperor, and the matter was handed over to the Ministry of War.  Wu Yuan Cui告 Shangshu Shi Xing said: This is a phrase from the Yougui Ji opera, how can it be used as evidence? Show the book from the market, and the Shangshu was relieved."

According to this, the person who pointed out that these two lines of poetry are from the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion was Wu Yuan Cui. Wu once wrote Linju Manlu, but unfortunately I have not been able to read it. The inaugural issue of the Peking University History Journal has Zhang Jun's reading notes, which also mentions this matter in the Manlu. But I don't know what the details of the original book are? In the Qing Dynasty, Chu Renhuo's Jianhu Ji also has the same narrative, but it is more detailed:

"In the year Yiwei of Wanli, the people of Wu were all cautious because Guanbai was not yet pacified. Wang Fengzhou's second son Shi Lu, Yanling Qin Fangbo Yao, younger brother Deng, and Qiao Xian's eldest son Xiang of Yunjian were all proud of their noble status. Shi inherited his ability to write articles, Deng was good at talking, and Xiang was good at calligraphy, each with a reputation at the time, and they interacted with each other, entering and exiting the narrow streets. When they met the sea police, they all rolled up their sleeves and stood up, as if they were about to say: I will quell the Japanese pirates, I will establish unprecedented merits. At that time, the traitor Zhao Zhouping, hiding among the young masters, used them to make himself important. He always wore a sword and traveled to wine shops and gambling places, and was always with the young masters. For a time, everyone knew Zhao Zhouping. He casually threw a thorn at the rich man, saying: We want to start something, pacify the island bandits, and lend your family a thousand gold to inlay. The rich man was afraid, or lent him a hundred gold, or dozens of gold, otherwise he would often stare at him and say: You guard the gold for me, I will soon lead troops to quell you! The intention was to get the gold, so I made big words to scare them. The rich men saw him interacting with the young masters, and often wore a sword in and out, thinking that he would soon lead his party to rob me of gold, and shouted that Zhao Zhouping, Wang, Qi, Qiao and the young masters were about to rebel. The Inspector Zhu Jiantang (Hongmo) ordered the yamen to arrest and punish them, and reported the matter to the court. The memorial contained anti-poetry, with the sentence "You really have the heart to chase Ji Bu, but the humble home has no way to entrust Zhu Jia." It was handed over to the Ministry of War for discussion, and Wu Ningfang (Cui) said to the Minister of War Shi Xing: These two sentences are from the Yougui Ji, how can they be used as evidence? It was handed over to the Pacification Commissioner to investigate, question, and found nothing. After that, the essay on Zhouping and the death of Deng, Shi embroidered the border, and Xiang was assigned. People all thought it was a wrong. The case of suspicion was detained for a long time. (Omitted below)."

Probably because of the times, there was no need to be taboo, so the record of the facts was clearer than Shen's. Only the year was Yiwei, two years later than Shen's record. In these three notes, all said that the two anti-poetry lines were in the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion. Although Linju Manlu has not been seen, it is expected that Wu Yuan Cui's own record, the resolver, will not be an exception. So here comes the question! In the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion, there really is no such poem. Not only is it not in the versions circulating now, but in Shen Defu's day, he had already "checked all the new and old carvings" and deeply changed his suspicions. In Guqu Zayan, there is the phrase "Qingsui Dingyou", which should have been written in the 25th year of Wanli (1597), only five years away from Gui Si; if it is based on Chu's theory as Yiwei, then it is only less than three years. Shen and Wang Fangzhong are also friends. Even Shen has checked the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion and "there is no such couplet", which seems to be a surprising thing.

Recently, I accidentally discovered that this poem was actually seen in the Ming Dynasty opera novel Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool, which also narrates the story of Jiang Shilong. This poem is loaded in the Xingshu in the first chapter, which can be obtained at the beginning of the volume, but a few numbers have been changed slightly

"Meeting like duckweed from the ends of the earth, literature and martial arts are outstanding, but prosperity should not be extravagant. The enemy country has the heart to chase Ji Bu, but the humble home has no courage to be Zhu Jia. How can a dragon be a thing in a pond, and jewels will eventually become flowers on brocade. From here, where you hold hands with Yi, the Kuibi shines on Jianghua."

According to Zheng Zhenduo's Pinghua Collection of the Ming and Qing Dynasties and Sun Kaidi's Preface to the Chinese Novel Catalogue Seen in Tokyo, Japan, the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool can be found in the Xiu Gu Chun Rong and Guo Se Tian Xiang two books, which also collect the Legendary Romance and Milian Ji. Except for this, it seems that it has not been recorded. What I saw was the lithographic edition of Shanghai Jinji Bookstore in the 20th year of Guangxu, Collection of Talents, which is the seven kinds published under Guo Se Tian Xiang, with the same order of headings. The first article is this Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool. The narrated plot is mostly taken from the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion. Wang Ruilan is Huang Ruilan, and her father's name is Huang Fu (ancestor Huang Qianshan) Tuo Man Xingfu is Pu Lu Xingfu, Jiang and Huang are not Jin people, but Song people, and Xingfu is a Jin fugitive general. It begins by describing the conclusion with Jiang, based on the cited poem above. The following customs have added a lot of embellishments, focusing on poetry and prose, and some empty arguments, full of opera literature. "Orchid Gathering Dragon Pool" is because Shilong drew this picture to convey it to Ruilan and plan to reunite. The most exciting and touching Moon-Worshipping section in the opera was deleted, and replaced with the scene of Jiang and Huang worshiping the moon in the eastern courtyard during their journey, which is really buying sandalwood and returning the pearl. Among them, Shilong's discussion of Liyuan's acting section mentioned the Jinyin Bayi Ji, etc. The era of writing should not be too early, always at the time of Long and Wan. Now I know that the first edition of the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool, Xiu Gu Chun Rong, was carved during the Wanli period.

Now we can base on this and have the following possible explanations for the "anti-poetry" incident:

1. The original text of the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion should have no such poem. At that time, people because the two characters of legend contain two kinds of literary styles, and the narrative is the same as Jiang Shilong's story, without detailed examination, it was transmitted as Yougui Ji, and it is unknown? The certified Fang edition may be the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool. If the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion hated the implication, and the subsequent editions were deleted by the Fangjia, then in Shen's time, the old version should not have been without it either.

2. Shen's words "the resolver pretended to say this" may be close to the facts. Wu Yuan Cui was also a Wu native. At that time, the fellow villagers of Suzhou tried their best to run for this great prison, which is a very obvious fact. (Such as Wang Xideng, etc.) The Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool was specially made for this matter, so the opening is this poem, for fear that people will not see it, and to prove that it came from the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion in a far-fetched way. The Moon-Worshipping Pavilion has been passed down for a long time and is difficult to attribute to it; the two characters of legend can be borrowed appropriately. However, most people know less about the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool, and there is still no doubt that it is the Moon-Worshipping Pavilion opera. Shen's record may still be intentionally concealing this loophole, and the tone of the so-called "hating the implication and cutting out some sentence" is originally more focused on the resolver's statement of "is that so"

3. In the poetry, the characters of opera are changed from "Junshi" to "Chouguo", and "No way" is changed to "No courage". In terms of the meaning of the text, there are fewer words that are violated, and the meaning is more careful and prudent. (The nationality of Jiang and Huang, changing Jin to Song, and changing Xingmian to Jin fugitive general, may be due to the fact that it is cut from the two characters of "Chouguo".) Although it is said late, this series of texts should be completely consistent with the records of Shen, Tan, and Chu; but Shen Ji's "Zuo" is the word "Tuo", and the three articles also have small differences. The differences between the few characters may not cause the above inferences to be overturned.

4. If we say this, the poetry contained in the Record of the Orchid Gathering at the Dragon Pool is no different from that of Shen, Tan, and Chu. "Chouguo" and so on were changed due to fear of disaster after this incident occurred. Then the era of writing this opera should be advanced a little earlier. The second argument is close to conjecture, and the first explanation may still be applicable

5. The results of the few parties involved in this public case seem to have not been exempted from guilt. The argumentation of the resolver has not had much effect. The Moon-Worshipping Pavilion probably has no such poem at all, but it is a fact of decorating words and making suggestions, and the authorities have already understood it later?

Crossing the Wu River (Part 1) 227

— You Gong

The days passed by hurriedly, what remained in the mind was like yesterday, but, that has already been three years of time!

It was the hottest time of the Great Heat, perhaps the roads of the city were melting with oil, cicada-wing gauze clothing had long been draped over the shoulders, but, in this mountain hollow, those things were nowhere to be seen. The hot stone blocks of the mountain path turned up the heat, penetrating leather shoes, trampling the soles of feet soaked in sweat. The head wouldn't feel comfortable either, the sun stared with blood-red eyes, making everyone's body feel a little prickly, a hat as big as a bamboo basket covered the forehead, but, when you stood in the deep shade of a tree and took off your hat, a rush of heat would rise straight from the crown of your head.

However, at this moment, joy seized our hearts, we breathed a long sigh towards the blue sky with floating cotton clouds. We thought, your blood-red eyes will have no power to glare anymore, the fences you have woven, from today on, we will destroy them all.

Truly, this is a miracle, like discovering a large clear spring in a desolate desert, we have been traveling on the sweltering mountain roads for a full eight days since leaving the pier. Although "cars" are not considered rare, perhaps as common as crawling stinkbugs in the city, but, being surrounded by mountains, to actually see these clean Ford cars, the joy can be clearly seen on our faces.

As usual, we got up at "the rooster's crow to see the sky," washed our faces in a flurry, this time, there was no need to bind the sedan chairs, and the luggage was all moved and loaded onto the long-distance bus. I don't know why, there were so many people, surrounding the car in a circle, muttering, looking around, smiling, the expressions were very complicated, later, probably thinking that this was still not enough, so, some honked the horn in front of the car, some touched the lights in front of the car, and even more pressed the tires hidden underneath. Is it laughable? Perhaps, a mountain city that cannot see the material civilization of the metropolis, how could it not arouse their sense of novelty?

Rushing out of the city, driving towards the relatively wider road. The road was not very smooth, the stones buried underneath were looking up, naturally, the car refused to stop bouncing, although avoiding the direct attack of the blood-red eyes, but, the wooden benches inside the car, sitting for a long time will also make the buttocks burn. Moreover, you have to be careful of your head, arms, shoulders, if you are not careful, maybe the wooden wall of the car will kiss you, making you burn with an unnamed fire under the sweet kiss.

——Thirty for big stations, fifteen for small stations. The wrinkles on Zhang Futou's forehead were moving again and again.

Introducing "A Famous Artist" 228

— Fang Turen

From the TASS news, I learned that the Soviet Union has been enthusiastically celebrating the fiftieth birthday of the genius playwright Belotserkovsky recently, and the chairman of the Central Committee of the country has decided to give him the honorary title of "Famous Artist." The name of this famous artist, as well as his masterpieces, are probably still very unfamiliar to readers in our country. Now, taking advantage of his fiftieth birthday, I will briefly introduce him with a few words, I hope readers will not blame me for being presumptuous.

Belotserkovsky worked as a sailor on Russian and English sailboats, as a factory worker on the European continent, as a farm laborer and a short-term worker in the Americas, and as a soldier in Siberia during the Russian Revolution. We can see his shadow in almost every upsurge of anger in Russia.

His plays reflect this very active and colorful life. "Response" describes how, during the period when Russia was subjected to armed intervention, American workers attempted to strike and refuse to transport munitions for the Allied countries. "The Moon Rises from the Left" is a love story during a turbulent period, famous for the line of the protagonist in the play: "Men and women who fall in love are counter-revolutionaries." "Storm" is his first revolutionary romance, and it is to show "the heroism of collective emotion." "Calm Waters" describes how the same characters in "Storm" continued to experience the New Economic Policy period. There are also many plays depicting sailors, plays depicting miners, and "Cage" cleverly depicts three eras of slavery: the black slaves on the coast of Africa that he saw from English sea vessels - almost like livestock; the serfs of old Russia; and the so-called modern slaves who unknowingly sold themselves - the cheapest slaves.

His early plays were all written for soldiers in Siberia. It was not until the performance of "Storm" in 1925 that he was called the first new playwright. He felt that the stage at that time was very conservative, and only entertained itself with classical heroes and bourgeois aesthetics. Artists and directors did not pay attention to new heroes; they did not come into contact with reality, and the characters in "Storm" were very novel and incredible to the actors at that time. When they first appeared on stage, it was as if elementary school students were reciting lessons they did not understand. However, the audience understood and cheered loudly, and at this time, the actors glimpsed the great significance of the "Storm" they were performing.

"Storm" is not only regarded as the first great Soviet tragedy, but also the most basic Soviet tragedy. It is a psychological study of the philosophical issues of life, death, and love. Through another lens of the microscope, the inner life of the creators of the new environment is examined. The love in the play arises naturally from the environment, and the sorrow is not the old-fashioned bourgeois hysteria. The new person feels in a new way, and this is not due to his nervous system, but to the basic position and the indomitable main action. All the characters are depicted as typical of their era in the sum of their lives. Everyone has his personal philosophy, but the personal philosophy is the representative of his collective philosophy.

"Storm" made Belotserkovsky a "Famous Artist." There is a special reason for this, and it is not accidental.

University Days (15) 229

— Written by German Storm, Translated by Chen Yinzhi

When I was fully awake, I was already lying on the sofa in the miller's house, the miller lived near the mill pond. Nali followed her mother home, her mother also came out of the city that day. Christopher stayed here, the miller's wife taught him, and he was busy putting damp bandages on my head. When I opened my eyes, he was sitting on a chair next to me, with a basin of water placed between his knees. He was about to change the bandage; but he now pulled his hand back, and he asked me timidly, "Can I help you, Philip?"

I sat up, trying to put my thoughts together, my head was aching badly. "No," I said after a while, "I don't need you to help."

"Shall I call someone from the city to come here?"

"You go; I can walk home myself."

Christopher hesitated and stood up, putting the basin on the table.

Soon after, the door of the room echoed, he grabbed the doorknob, but he didn't leave. When I turned back to look, I saw my old friend's eyes with an expression of sincere sorrow looking at me.

I still hesitated for a second. "Christopher," I said, stood up and held out my hand to him, "If you have free time, then please stay a little longer, you can take my arm to support me, and we will walk back to the city together."

His face shone with joy. He grabbed my hand and shook it. "That punch was too heavy, Philip!" he said.

Reviving the Nation and Transforming the People 230

— Xing An

Our nation has long been known as the "sick man of East Asia," which is a great shame! Now, Mr. Chen Lifu, Mr. Cai Yuanpei, and Mr. Yu Youren, in view of the weakness and decline of the entire nation's physiology and behavior, in order to revive the nation, have initiated and organized a National Transformation Society to study the nation's pathological conditions and seek transformation strategies. They are now actively preparing and have issued an organizational declaration and transformation plan. In the declaration, it is pointed out that the physiological state of our nation is a group of people with a hundred diseases. Such as hunchbacks and shrugged shoulders, weak spirits, many sickly and deformed conditions, a frowning and pale complexion, slow movements, lack of work intensity, withered and lifeless, old and decrepit, men lack the air of beards and eyebrows, and women still have a worried and sickly appearance. Throughout the country, regardless of wisdom or foolishness, none are free from a dull and lifeless atmosphere. As for behavioral pathologies, they include starting strong but finishing weakly, enthusiasm only five minutes, perfunctory, hypocritical, and unity seeming like loose sand, with vision as small as a grain of sand. The plan they have formulated is for the government to concentrate the strength of the entire nation to seek the construction of the north, striving to achieve the goal of prosperity. At the same time, the government should gradually develop the north and attract back the excellent people who have migrated south. Furthermore, scientific methods should be used to implement marriage control. Other methods, such as food, disease, and other methods to save physical and mental health, should also be scientifically controlled.

To strengthen a country, one must first strengthen its people. Without a strong nation, hoping for a prosperous country is nothing but a fool's dream. The weakness and decline of our entire nation is an undeniable phenomenon. The solution must start with transforming the people, and with the united efforts of the whole country in all aspects, we must ensure that our 400 million people achieve balanced intellectual and physical development. When the voice of national revival spreads throughout the country, the organization of this National Transformation Society by our country's intellectuals is truly something for the people to celebrate!

However, today, talking about reviving the nation and transforming the people, although urgent, the work of transforming the people is very difficult. Because the weakness and decline of our nation has been going on for a long time, to transform it cannot be achieved in a day or two. It is necessary for the entire country to devote all its efforts to hope for success. In my personal opinion, transforming the people should start from two aspects. One aspect is the transformation of the national spirit, transforming the negative, corrupt, conservative, superstitious, timid, selfish, narrow-minded, and regressive spirit of our nation into a positive, fresh, trendy, scientific, courageous, generous, and progressive spirit. The most powerful and effective method of transforming the spirit is education. I hope that those engaged in education will pay attention to this and take on the responsibility of transforming the nation!

The other aspect is the transformation of physical fitness. The weakness of our nation's physical fitness, like the decline of our spirit, has almost become incurable, truly a group of people with a hundred diseases. If we do not seek to transform this national physical fitness early, even if others do not destroy us in the future, we will destroy ourselves! And a sound mind resides in a sound body. Without transforming physical fitness, hoping for a sound spirit is impossible. Therefore, transforming physical fitness is more important than transforming the spirit. But how to transform physical fitness? The most important thing is to promote physical education. We must enable people throughout the country, regardless of men, women, old, or young, farmers, workers, merchants, or soldiers, to practice beneficial exercises to forge their physical fitness and become a physically strong nation. Secondly, the selection of spouses and the birth of children should also be carefully considered. As for daily life, diet, hygiene, diseases, etc., we must pay full attention to them. These are also very important to the physical fitness of the nation.

The rise and fall of the nation depends on this one action. May our people rise up and devote themselves to the transformation of the nation!

A Record of Welcome Rain 231

— Ye Fei

Last year's great drought dealt a great blow to the countryside, but there was no snow in winter, and not much rain in spring; all the way to Grain Full, the heavens were still dry and did not send down water. The fields were as dry as red soil, the ponds only had bottom water left, and the silt and beaches of the riverbanks all appeared on the surface to compete with the scorching sun, even the few deeper canals only had a thin layer of melon peel water. So the farmers felt a dreaded horror in their hearts, a second drought was about to come!

Time passed with the rise and fall of the thermometer, and in the blink of an eye, Grain in Ear had passed, and the high and low fields should have been preparing for transplanting rice seedlings; but in many places, the fields were plowed roughly, but the soil was as hard as iron, and there was no ankle-deep water in the field ditches. If the sky didn't send down some water, then how could the seedlings be transplanted? If we waited another ten days or so, the time for transplanting seedlings would pass, and then even if water came, it would be too late; if this continued, could this year's drought be avoided?

In a few places near rivers and canals with water, water was being pumped day and night, but those dry and cursed fields could only stare at the sky with wide eyes, with seedlings but no place to plant them, but the lowland fields were not good either, planting Indica rice would mean fearing that the sky would not rain, so it would still be a dry death, if planting late rice, then when the autumn began, it would be pouring with reverse plum rain, inevitably being flooded, so this year the high fields were not good, and the low fields were also annoying, truly making the farmers anxious and unable to think of a solution. Especially Desheng's father at the head of Wu Village, these days he has been restless like an ant on a hot pot, and now, in the name of the village elder, he has convened an emergency meeting in the Shen family ancestral hall:

"If the sky continues to be so dry, we will definitely not be able to plant our seedlings this year; we have already suffered a drought last year, and if we have another year like that this year, then can we common people bear it? Now is the time to plant seedlings but no water comes, what use will it be if it comes later? I think now that time is urgent, we should immediately notify the village tomorrow to first abstain from killing livestock, and if it doesn't rain again in a week, we will have to trouble the Five Saints God and ask him to come out to pray for rain." Desheng's father sat at the head of the table and expressed his opinion, then knocked out the ashes from his pipe, took a sip of tea to moisten his throat, and asked everyone again: "What do you all think?"

Their meeting didn't have any formalities, they just put two square tables together in the dining hall of the ancestral hall, placed more than ten benches around, and had a pot of tea and a few packs of old yellow cigarettes prepared, and everyone sat there in a chaotic manner to discuss.

After Desheng's father finished speaking, he used a pair of bright eyes to sweep over everyone's faces.

"Yes, what the old man said is right, we should first abstain from killing livestock starting tomorrow." Everyone answered in unison.

"Ah! I have lived for more than fifty years, and I have never encountered such a year, if the people don't do evil, how can the heavens send down so many disasters?" Desheng's father stood up, walked out of the circle of conversation, and sighed like this.

But when they dispersed from the meeting and were about to walk out of the ancestral hall door, dark clouds had already gathered in the sky.

Page 20

. Before they had returned home, copper coin-sized raindrops had already hit the earth; in less than an hour, several ditches were gurgling with rapid streams, and an inch of water had accumulated in the fields.

The rain didn't stop all day, and it continued until the morning of the next day. The villagers, with pale faces, all showed a layer of gratified smiles. At this time, everyone put on bamboo hats, draped on straw raincoats, and went to work in the fields—transplanting seedlings.

"This rain, although not very heavy, is already our life-saving water, as long as it can rain again in a few days, and continue like this, then there is hope!" Desheng's father finished transplanting the seedlings, walked out of the field, and when he sat on the field ridge to rest, he smoked his pipe while looking at the sky and saying.

"Yes! We always need the help of the Heaven God, only then will we poor people have a life!" Little Tou San lazily stood up from the ground, stretched, and felt that the field work these days was too heavy, so his limbs were as tired as if they were paralyzed, but his spirit was excited.

Half a month later, a large area of fields near Wu Village Head was covered with lush green rice seedlings, swaying happily in the wind under the drizzle or sunny days.

Fleeing the Famine 232

— Lin Hao

Here, in the advent of the Plum Rain season, a flood broke out, and it was only with great difficulty that it receded not long after; thus, the nourishment for sustaining life here was completely devoured, leaving behind some people, some people as hungry as ghosts.

Needless to say, the mud was swollen like cotton, gnawing at people's toes, the tree trunks were also covered with mud, and the fields had lost their traces. Truly, a small and densely populated village ten days ago is now as desolate as a withered temple, no, a vast desert.

Night gradually eroded the light; the wounded village could not find a trace of light. Everyone, with empty stomachs, cursed their fate in the dark territory. The sky and the sky ten days ago had not changed, still the same bright moon, still the same twinkling stars; but, in this group of poor lives, they felt a world of difference from ten days ago. They didn't understand what kind of evil people were committing this year? The suffering in the world was already felt to be unbearable, and with such an incurable natural disaster, it symbolized the descent of the end and the premonition of the extinction of life!

So, everyone held such a terrifying soul.

Fortunately, it was the scorching summer, and sleeping in the open air at night didn't feel very cold. Coupled with everyone's enthusiasm, they didn't feel lonely. When the food was cut off, everyone asked the famous wise man—Chen Laoguan. In such a mood, Chen Laoguan could no longer think of a solution: "Ah! What about the food in the future?"

"Isn't it? Such a big group of people!" Ah Gui's father added.

You looked at me, I looked at you, everyone couldn't think of any clues. Finally, it was the teacher Wang who said such a passage: "Isn't waiting for death here staring at the mud? The only way is to go to the provincial capital."

"That's right, what teacher Wang said is right." Chen Laoguan said.

"Then, without delay, let's leave early tomorrow morning!"

"Okay, let's leave tomorrow." Everyone said so.

The stars twinkled, as if mocking.

The night was further stripped away, and it was almost impossible to see even the faces of people a foot away. After a compromised decision, everyone tightened their belts, hid an empty stomach, and wearily lay across the only remaining broken mats to pass the night.

Quietly, occasionally a weak dog barked in the distance, which would make these frightened people open their tired eyes. To see if there were any changes.

The children cried out in hoarse little throats because they had no milk to eat: the women sang sad lullabies, and the men sighed. In peacetime, they would have been asleep in dreamland. But today, for some reason, they didn't even have the mood to doze off. Cries, lullabies, sighs, as well as the light barks of dogs and the calls of night owls, harmonized into (the most famous sad song in the world.

The night was spent in a bleak atmosphere.

The next day, in the early morning when the stars had not yet disappeared, the sky was still stained with a dark gray hue. The impatient Huang Dasao shouted: "It's not early! We should get up and prepare our things, and hurry to the provincial capital!"

Without nostalgia, without sadness, everyone got up in a swarm, and packed some broken things. The men put the children in baskets and carried them on poles, the women carried some broken cloth clothes and cotton wool on their backs, and the elderly supported their weak bodies and stepped step by step on the way to their future.

The sun rose, willfully inflicting a severe torture on everything of the people, the fire also seemed to burn out sweat drops on people's backs. The earth was like being poured with boiling water, so hot that it hurt the soles of their feet. Two

A skinny dog, stretched out its tongue tip, greedily lowered its head and kissed the ground.

Movie News

A Casual Discussion on "Autumn Fan Lamp Light" 238

"Autumn Fan Lamp Light" adopts extremely realistic themes to depict the social pathology—the problem born from the interweaving of feudalism and new romantic ideas.

The playwright Tan Youliu does not just sympathize with those who are sacrificed under social pathology, but also strongly points out the reactions that these people should have after being stimulated by social pathology.

A purely feudal father, a daughter endowed with the ability to scout out the opposite sex and infected with new ideas, and a self-abandoning youth, and a woman who lives a distorted life without realizing it, perform the tragedy of temptation, abandonment, and depravity that society has seen.

"Autumn Fan Lamp Light" not only thoroughly reveals the development and end of this tragedy, but more valuable is that it portrays the resurrection process of the protagonists of this tragedy and the motivation for seeking rebirth.

Tan Youliu used special techniques, calmly describing the story, and clearly organizing the pictures, which strengthened the central structure of "Autumn Fan Lamp Light", and loudly appealed to people who were lost, pointing out the path to light.

A person's life is dead, there is no possibility of resurrection, a person's soul has fallen, there is a chance of rebirth, and a strong will can break social discrimination and strengthen the self-confidence of those who seek rebirth.

Li Lili has always played cheerful and lively roles in her plays. In "Autumn Fan Lamp Light", she has to play a sad, melancholy, dignified play, which is completely different from before. Her success in this change of style determines that she is a multifaceted role.

Diao Banhua, a new star who has already attracted special attention, "Autumn Fan Lamp Light" is her first leading role in the film industry. Her unique talent and unique acting skills have not only won this special opportunity, but also won special success to satisfy the audience's hopes and high demands.

Shang Guanwu played the traitor Hu Fu in "The Road" and the lecherous gentry He Renzhai in "Fisherman's Song". In the future "Tian Lun", he also plays another different role, none of which are not well-acted. In "Autumn Fan Lamp Light", he plays a rigid feudal father, and his acting skills have developed to a new path.

Gu Menghu, who won praise in "New Woman", plays one of the protagonists, the depraved youth, and Huang Yunzhen also plays the type of role she specializes in, which are undoubtedly satisfying to the audience.

Of course, the success of a film is not only determined by the success of the screenwriter, director and leading actors, but also by the help of other aspects.

Half a Week in the Sky 240

Shenbao Architectural Weekly

The Process of Architecture and Building Materials in This City (II) 241

— Gu Ying

Timber imports increased by 4 million in the first four months of this year compared with the same period last year. Cement imports have only remained at one-fifth of what they were three years ago since the implementation of the new tax.

2. Timber

Chinese domestic timber is called Guang timber, Xi timber, Jian timber, Hang timber, etc. Guang timber has the richest production, originating in northern Guangxi, eastern Guizhou, and between the Five Ridges and Hengshan Mountains of Hunan. Because its reserves are the deepest, its annual output is the most abundant. Next are Xi timber, Jian timber, and Hang timber, etc., whose annual output is similar. Xi timber is produced in the Shanling and Jiulian Mountains in Jiangxi. Due to the constant entry and exit of the communists and the continuous warfare, there is a lack of cultivation, and production has sharply decreased. Jian timber is produced in Jianning, Jianou, etc. in Fujian. Its production is mostly in sections, such as the double, half, barrel, and single wood sold in this city. Hang timber is produced in various counties in western Zhejiang, coming out along the Qujiang and Huijiang rivers, and gathering in Hangzhou (hence the name). However, the properties of the timber produced in the two rivers are different. The timber produced in the Qujiang area is naturally old, gentle, and hard. The timber produced in the Huijiang area is easily grown through artificial cultivation, and the output is more abundant, but its nature is loose and tender, far less than that produced in the Qujiang area. Those who operate in this industry flourished most in 1925 and 1926. The annual sales in this city were always as high as 30 to 40 million yuan. Recently, because town architecture has trended towards Europeanization to reduce pillars, long materials are needed, so Chinese people are happy to use foreign timber, because Chinese timber is not as large as foreign timber. Therefore, except for rural architecture and small buildings using Chinese timber, such as the tall buildings in towns and the sleepers used on railways, there is no one that does not use foreign pine. The sales of Chinese timber have sharply decreased, and the import of foreign timber has increased year by year. According to customs reports, the import of timber from January to April this year reached 9,218,775 customs gold units, equivalent to 15,883,949 national currency units. Compared with 5,020,597 customs gold units in the same period last year, it increased by 83% in terms of customs gold. If compared with the import volume of 4,894,622 customs gold units in the same period in 1933, the import volume in the same period of 1936 increased by 90%. A table is listed below.

The Magnificent Appearance of the New Welfare Company Building 242

General Overview of the New Welfare Company Building 243

— Yun

Welfare Company is one of the famous department stores at sea. It has been established for many years and has developed its business and enjoys a good reputation. Now, in order to expand its business, the company has built a new building at 190-208 Jing'an Temple Road, which has been completed and moved in. It will open for business on Wednesday, July 3rd. Here is a brief description of the new building! The new Welfare building is located near the International Hotel and the Grand Bright Cinema, directly opposite the Racecourse. The location is suitable, and the architecture is beautiful. From the perspective of buyers, it is truly a magnificent department store. The Welfare Company's own buildings include the ground floor, the second floor, and the third floor. The upper two floors are new-style apartments. The internal location of the new building needs to be expanded as much as possible, and at the same time, it is necessary to avoid using too many pillars. Therefore, the architects, Cass 洋行, and their engineer, Mr. Bao Lisu Lebosiji, have put a lot of effort into this. After using arches with a span of 75 feet to support these two floors of apartments, the fourth floor can be absolutely pillar-free. According to the 6,000 to 7,000 square feet location, but can not use pillars, this is still a new idea in Shanghai. The arch with a span of 75 feet to support the building, is not common. The towering part of the façade of the new building is equipped with neon lights by Li'an Electric Company, which shines brightly at night, adding to the spectacle. The new building was built by Senji Construction Factory, the elevator was installed by Xiangtai, the plumbing and heating equipment were contracted by Maoli, and the lighting equipment was contracted by Shenchang 洋行. It is also heard that in order to facilitate customers, the company has not only hired many Chinese assistants to serve sincerely, but also set up a parking lot near the company for customers to park their vehicles at any time. The parking lot is located next to the small vegetable market in the Racecourse. Cars can be driven in from Jing'an Temple Road and Baker Road. The distance between the field and the new Welfare building is only a short distance, and when vehicles are parked there, there are guards on duty to watch closely, so it can be guaranteed that there will be no obstacles.

Shenbao Architecture Special Issue Department

The Design of the Latest American Theaters (Middle) 244

— Original by B. A. Hueton, Translated by Xiao Ang

(II) Selection of Architectural Style

The form of the theater is closely related to the business. If the form is exquisite, it can attract the attention of pedestrians and be beautiful, and the business will definitely be prosperous. But the theater is a place for high-end entertainment, so it must be very magnificent and elegant. Russian theaters noticed this point very early. This time, Mr. Hueton introduced this style to the United States.

(III) Internal Design

(A) Lounge. Before the movie starts, there must be many viewers waiting in front of the door, so the lounge is indispensable. The equipment here may be a little luxurious, and the furnishings may be a little noble. There are sofas, coffee points, and toilets. In short, it is necessary to prevent the audience from feeling the wait. The place here can be larger, able to accommodate one-third of the audience. There is heating in winter and electric fans in summer. At the same time, very beautiful photos of stars and very moving advertisements can be hung on the walls. These are closely related to the business and must be paid attention to.

(B) Line of Sight. The most important thing in the design of the theater is the line of sight. Whether upstairs, downstairs, or in the corners, you must be able to see clearly. This is a very difficult problem to solve. Mr. Haueton can use his genius to change the shape of the theater into a particularly suitable oval shape according to the principles of optics. The focal point of the movie machine is at this end, and the focal point of the screen is at that end. In this way, the light is reflected out, and the audience in the four seats feels particularly clear and comfortable. This is his amazing discovery and creation.

(C) Sound Waves - The second most important thing is sound waves. Now that sound movies have been invented, the sound must be particularly clear and pleasant. There must be echoes to increase the sound, and at the same time, there must be sound-absorbing materials to make the sound even. Mr. Haoton's use of the focal point's position has resulted in a particularly good sound, which can be said to be an extraordinary success.
